Roosevelt Searches for Cabinet Members 74

Most Important People Cannot Enter the Cabinet

Reuters, New York, 3rd - When Roosevelt was elected President, the people harbored a kind of fantasy, believing that outstanding talents such as Young, Baruch, Lees, Davis, Baker, and Tralle would all join the cabinet. If any three of the aforementioned individuals were to take on three key positions, the new cabinet would present a unique atmosphere. However, according to current news, the possibility of their entering the cabinet is gradually diminishing. The difficulties felt by the previous president are now also felt by Mr. Roosevelt. The great figures of a country each have good reasons why they cannot hold cabinet positions, whether due to business or health, they cannot devote themselves to public service. Moreover, three of the aforementioned six people reside in New York. Mr. Roosevelt has already chosen his campaign director, Farley, to be the Postmaster General of the new cabinet. Farley is from New York, so Mr. Roosevelt can only choose one more person from New York to enter the cabinet. Furthermore, the decline in business is one reason why Mr. Roosevelt cannot freely choose people. People in the business world, in the current situation, feel that their own businesses require their constant attention. The banking world cannot leave banking for other pursuits, as Young is a case in point. For business reasons, Young cannot sacrifice the next four years in Washington politics. However, Young may accept a temporary appointment to handle negotiations regarding war debts. It is heard that Mr. Tralle cannot separate himself from banking either. If Mr. Roosevelt recruits Baker into the cabinet, he will inevitably break with publishing magnate Hearst, who did his best to help Mr. Roosevelt during the general election, wanting to avoid Baker being rejected as a presidential candidate. It is heard that Mr. Roosevelt intends to appoint New York lawyer Perkins as Secretary of Labor, opening a new era of women entering the cabinet. If Ms. Perkins and Farley are both cabinet members, then Mr. Roosevelt may not further woo other New Yorkers into the cabinet. Therefore, Davis and Baruch will both be unable to be listed on the cabinet member list, as both of them reside in New York.

Havas, London, 4th - According to a reporter from the Daily Telegraph stationed in Hot Springs, the future organization of the Roosevelt government is currently being measured from unofficial sources. The Secretary of State will be Senator Hull of Tennessee, the Secretary of the Treasury will be Senator Glass of Virginia, the Postmaster General will be Farley, and the Secretary of Labor will be Ms. Perkins. Ms. Perkins was born in Boston, Massachusetts in 1882 and is particularly qualified for the position of Secretary of Labor. Her sociological writings are quite reputable in the United States. Since 1910, she has held important positions in various industries. Mr. Roosevelt left Hot Springs by yacht last night but is still communicating with Miami City via wireless telephone and transmitting news to newspapers daily. Before setting sail, Mr. Roosevelt declared that the list of cabinet members would be announced on March 2nd and that he intended to convene a special session of Congress to balance the budget and adopt necessary resolutions on various issues that the Republican administration had slightly neglected or handed over for pending action.

U.S. Taxation is Also Not Unified 75

Hoover Strongly Advocates Reforming the System

National News, Washington, 3rd - Today, U.S. President Hoover gave a speech at the annual meeting of the American Legislators Association, urging reform of the national taxation system, eliminating overlapping taxation agencies to reduce waste and enrich the national treasury. This speech by Hoover is generally regarded as his last speech on economic matters during his term. It is said that at present, the U.S. federal government and various states, counties, and cities each have their own taxation systems, which are not connected. Even the budget plans, financial plans, and tax rates of each state are not reported to the federal government. Often, the federal government's taxation plans have already been implemented by various states, resulting in overlapping and substantial losses. Therefore, it is suggested that the states and the federal government should cooperate with each other to solve this problem scientifically. Currently, some towns often have four taxation agencies, which results in a significant loss in the efficiency of taxation. If these can be reorganized, waste can be greatly reduced and efficiency can be greatly increased.

Famous European Volcano Erupts 76

Reuters, Rome, 3rd - The famous Mount Vesuvius has now become active again. Shaking stones are shooting into the air, as dense as rain. Onlookers are all shocked and terrified, and earthquakes are rumbling. Residents in the surrounding area all fled their homes yesterday and camped out in the fields. So far, no losses have occurred. However, Professor Malaterra, director of the Vesuvius Observatory, has issued a serious warning, saying that the current intense eruption seems to be temporary, but the center of the volcano clearly has the brewing of a fierce eruption, which will reach the point of explosion sometime this spring. The professor also said that the vent of the current volcano is gradually shrinking. If it continues to shrink, then it may erupt a new vent as in 1929. In that year, the volcano's molten vent destroyed an entire town. The professor also predicted that this year's eruption will be far more intense than usual. It is found that the volcano has never been completely silent since the major eruption on August 24, 79 AD. Since then, it has erupted periodically. In 472 and 1631, the hot ash and gravel fell directly to Constantinople. In 51, it even reached Tripoli in Africa.

The Issue of a Japanese-Russian Non-Aggression Treaty (Tokyo Dispatch) 79

The Opinions of Supporters Deserve Attention

Since Japan's invasion of the three northeastern provinces, the war clouds over the Pacific have remained dense for a year. Japan is suffering from domestic economic panic and fearing the threats of Russian and American power. Manchuria, a piece of flesh, is likely to be difficult to swallow safely. Therefore, for half a year, the atmosphere of Japan and Russia concluding a non-aggression treaty has been propagated in the government and among the people, but the actual occurrence has been slow in coming. According to the conversation between Foreign Minister Uchida and newspaper reporters, although it is said that the borders of Japan, Russia, and Manchuria are intertwined and disputes can occur at any time, if a Japanese-Russian-Manchurian tripartite committee is established, it can be adjusted accordingly. Regarding the issue of this committee, representatives of the Russian and Japanese consulates in Harbin are discussing it accordingly. Once the newly appointed Japanese ambassador to Russia arrives in Moscow, the Russian and Japanese governments can begin formal negotiations on this matter. However, recently, small red and white leaflets have been discovered, printed in Russian and Japanese, demanding severance of relations with Soviet Russia. From this, it can also be seen that the Japanese people have a deep aversion to Russia, and the talk of a treaty may be difficult to achieve in practice.

However, Japanese people have extremely inconsistent views on the issue of Japan and Russia concluding a non-aggression treaty. Some are extremely opposed to concluding, while others are trying their best to support it. Here are the opinions of various parties on this issue, as reported here, summarized as follows: Some people say that Soviet Russia is communist, and Japan is a capitalist country. In terms of the national essence (the foundation of the country), Japan and Russia have absolutely no possibility of cooperation, and they should not cooperate. Furthermore, based on this viewpoint, Japan must attack Soviet Russia because Japan is taking advantage of this once-in-a-lifetime opportunity to use Manchuria as a foothold to erect the banner of eliminating the proletarian dictatorship of the communist country. On the one hand, it can win the sympathy of capitalist powers such as Britain, the United States, France, Italy, and Germany, and at the same time, it can make the "Manchukuo" obtain world recognition, overcome the League of Nations, overcome China, and easily "finish" the Manchurian issue. On the other hand, since the revolution, Soviet Russia has been painstakingly engaged in domestic economic construction, making great efforts of blood and flesh. Now, the five-year plan is yet to be completed, and the manufacture of domestic armaments has not yet reached perfection. Therefore, its diplomatic policy in recent years has reversed its previous revolutionary and tough diplomacy, and has quickly shifted to peaceful diplomacy. It can be seen that what Soviet Russia needs most today is to ease diplomatic relations, be honest and friendly, and work hard to build national strength. If Japan does not take advantage of a quick victory, it is feared that the strength of the Soviet Union will gradually expand in the future, and there will be an irreversible situation.

Among the members of the Seiyukai, internal opinions on the matter of Japan and the Soviet Union concluding a non-aggression treaty are also very different. The Japanese Foreign Ministry itself also has its own arguments on this matter, and they do not agree with each other. Supporters mostly say that the closer the relationship between Japan and Russia, the greater the benefits Japan can obtain. Opponents use the spread of communist ideology to Japan as an excuse. However, both sides currently have no good feelings towards Soviet Russia because Moscow published documents on this matter without paying attention to Japan's request not to publish it temporarily, and the Japanese Foreign Minister believes that there are insulting words in the note from the Russian ambassador to Japan.

In addition, there is another school of thought that is most peculiar and can be called the fence-sitters because they acknowledge the benefits of concluding a treaty on the one hand, and fear the spread of communist ideology in the country on the other. Therefore, the conclusion of this school of thought is that it is beneficial for us (referring to Japan) to conclude a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty, but unfortunately, the timing is not yet ripe and still needs to wait.

Finally, we will elaborate on the arguments of the supporters who promote the most and are proud of their clear views.

The supporters say that the existence of "Manchukuo" is an ironclad fact. However, the Manchurian issue has not yet reached the time for resolution internationally. Regardless of how the Manchurian issue will be resolved in the future, it is undoubtedly a critical juncture for the survival and prosperity of the Japanese nation. Therefore, when this issue is about to be resolved, the entire Japanese nation must exert all its strength. Studying the issue of concluding a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty from this point of view, especially at a time when diplomacy is in isolation, Japan cannot but express its support in order to extricate itself. Moreover, the conclusion of a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty has greater positive benefits for Japan, not just easing diplomacy. Indirectly, it can give Soviet Russia the opportunity to change direction. Directly, first, it can win over Soviet Russia to recognize "Manchukuo," and then the three countries of Japan, Manchuria, and Russia can cooperate with each other to continue to struggle in the international political situation for a long time. Second, obtaining Soviet Russia from outside the League of Nations circle can shift the international political situation in a way that is beneficial to Japan. Third, it can reduce the pressure from the United States on Japan. Fourth, it can make China's policy of alliance with Russia to contain Japan fall through. Ninth, trading with Soviet Russia can mutually benefit and increase economic benefits. Sixth, in the event of war between Japan and the United States, our country can also use this to shorten the defense line. After the conclusion of the Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty, the benefits obtained by Japan, although the supporters also have a lot of debate and disagreement, can mostly be included in the above points. Regarding the reasons for these points, some are very obvious and easy to understand and do not require explanation, while others require a little simple explanation. We may as well elaborate again. First, make Soviet Russia change direction. The reason held by Japanese war-against-Russia proponents is undoubtedly to prevent and contain the expansion of Soviet Russia's southward policy. Of course, going south is Russia's traditional policy, and it is true to say that Soviet Russia has not abandoned this attempt. However, Soviet Russia's southward expansion is not necessarily limited to the Far East. Supporters of the Japan-Russia treaty advocate that only the conclusion of a Japan-Russia non-aggression treaty is the driving force for making Soviet Russia change its policy to the West. The turning of Soviet Russia's policy to the East was still a relatively late matter, that is, after the Russo-Turkish War. Its previous southward policy was towards the Balkans and Central Asia. Later, due to the obstruction of Britain, France, and Germany, Soviet Russia turned its policy to the East, where the pressure was weak. This was the beginning of Soviet Russia's southward policy turning to the Far East. Subsequently, Britain, Germany, and France each took their own interests and encouraged Soviet Russia to maintain this diplomatic policy. However, since Soviet Russia changed its policy to the Far East, it has become opposed to Japan. Since the imperial government was overthrown and the revolutionary government came to power, it has turned its diplomatic activities, which used to be based in Europe, to the East. As a result, it has now clashed with Japan's iron wall once again (the Northeast Incident). Now, Soviet Russia has a southward trend in Central Asia, and railways are being built rapidly in the Caucasus, and economic progress is also being made step by step. On the other hand, the railway from Novosibirsk to Tashkent, crossing the Pamir Plateau, can go straight to India southward. Supporters say that the conclusion of a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty can make Russia's policy focus on these two aspects and abandon its attempt to go south in the Far East. At present, there are various difficulties in Soviet Russia's internal affairs, which is its weakness, so it has to try its best to avoid war, and whether it is temporary or expedient, it will always propose to me to conclude a non-aggression treaty. In the current international political situation, if Japan can obtain an absolutely favorable solution to the Manchurian issue, Japan's future development can be predicted. If there is any mistake in the solution to this issue, it goes without saying that the development on the mainland will be frustrated, and there is a risk of causing a domestic crisis in Japan. Moreover, at this moment, Soviet Russia's recognition of "Manchukuo" and Soviet Russia's other assistance to Japan are related to the solution of the Manchurian issue internationally. Now that Soviet Russia is proposing to me to conclude a non-aggression treaty because of internal difficulties, if we do not make good use of this good opportunity, I really do not understand how we can do well afterwards. (To be continued)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Limits Three Months to Eliminate Communist Bandits in Jiangxi 80

The Bandit Troops Have Abandoned Eastern Jiangxi and Retreated to the Fujian Border

Jiangxi People Visit Chiang Kai-shek to Express Assistance in Suppressing Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's visit to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression of bandits is indeed with full determination. Therefore, on the second day of arriving in Jiangxi, he gave a speech at the expanded memorial week meeting of the provincial party headquarters, stating that "The success or failure of this bandit suppression is related to the survival of the country and is also a touchstone for whether our nation can defend and strengthen itself. If the Jiangxi Red Bandits are not cleared, it is the responsibility of the government and myself, and it is also the shame of the people of Jiangxi. The requirements for suppressing the Red Bandits are, first, to be determined to have bandits or have me, and have me or have no bandits. Second, all party, government, and military agencies must be realistic and not superficially compliant. Third, the entire Jiangxi must be mobilized to cooperate as one, implement the creed of being practical, working hard, working solidly, and working quickly. It is necessary to cherish time, and the work of one day must be done in two days. Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the only weapons for suppressing bandits. We must lead by example to reverse the declining trend. Suppressing bandits, in particular, is to attack the mind. To attack the enemy's mind, we must first attack our own mind. Only in this way can we assume the responsibility of suppressing the Red Bandits and complete the task of suppressing the Red Bandits." From this, Chiang's intentions and strategies can be seen. As for the real strength of the bandit suppression, it is estimated to be more than 300,000 troops, which is more than ten times the bandit troops of the Zhu Mao pseudo-135th Army Corps. Therefore, the troops are sufficient for distribution, but the only problem lies in unified command and close coordination. Chiang paid special attention to this in order to encircle and annihilate the bandits. However, to avoid reality, the bandits withdrew from Dongxiang on the 25th, Xuwan on the 26th, Jinxi on the 28th, and the Zuofangying and Huangshidu areas of their base camp on the 29th and 30th. According to reports from the front line, the bandits have desperately retreated from Zixi and Lichuan to Jianning and Ninghua in western Fujian and Guangchang and Shicheng in southern Jiangxi, and will completely abandon eastern Jiangxi and retreat to the old nests in the mountains on the borders of Jiangxi and Fujian, fortifying their walls and clearing the fields to exhaust our troops, or make other plans along the borders of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong. From the current situation, the recovery of Zixi and Lichuan seems to be no problem. However, Chiang's visit to Jiangxi this time is not to drive the bandits away, but to annihilate the main force of the bandits in order to fundamentally eliminate them. Therefore, in addition to telegraphing Cai in Fujian, Chen in Guangdong, and Yu Hanmou, Liu Heding, Zhang Zhen, Liu Zhennian, Zhao Guantao, and other border area generals to jointly suppress bandits along the borders of Jiangxi and Fujian, he also telegraphed the front-line generals to the province to hold a military conference. The participants included Chen Cheng, commander-in-chief of the forward line, Sun Lianzhong, commander-in-chief of the 26th Route, Wu Qiwu, commander of the 4th Army, Li Mo'an, commander of the 10th Division, Luo Zhuoying, commander of the 11th Division, He Guoguang, chief of staff of the three provinces' headquarters, and senior personnel of the headquarters. The meeting was held from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM on the 31st of last month. The content is related to military plans and is still unknown. However, after the meeting, the generals returned to their defenses and supervised the advance of the troops. It is faintly heard that the various units with the 18th Army as the main force have arrived in Zixi, and the Li and Tao divisions in Liangnan are moving towards Lichuan. The Li Yunheng, Zhou Hunyuan, and Wang Jinwen divisions are advancing from Guixi towards the Fujian border in coordination. The divisions will further attack the Fujian border. The provincial air force has been flying to the Fujian border for reconnaissance and bombing for several days, and they are also very busy.

The gentry, farmers, merchants, students, women, and free professional groups in the province held a joint meeting at the Desheng Grand Theater on the 1st, with hundreds of organizations attending. A Jiangxi All-Circles Assistance Bandit Suppression Committee was established, and Zhou Guanhong and 27 others were elected as executive committee members. Fan Zhengbo, Xu Ruifu, Min Binru, Xia Jia, Yu Shukun, Ouyang Wu, and Peng Chengwan were appointed to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek together with Governor of Jiangxi Xiong Shihui to express assistance in suppressing bandits. Several Major Issues in the Draft Constitution 81

Sun Ke's Published Opinions

Beijing News: Recently, the people of the country have attached great importance to the drafting of the constitution. Regarding the most important points of the constitution, according to Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, opinions were published yesterday, recorded as follows:

Determining Principles 82

(Reporter asked) Has the Central Political Committee determined the principles of the draft constitution? (Sun Ke replied) The highest principle of the draft constitution is based on the legacy of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People and the Five-Power Constitution. The first step is for the Constitutional Drafting Committee of this Yuan to formulate an outline and submit it to the Central Political Committee to determine the drafting principles, and then submit it to this Yuan for group research. Each group will conduct in-depth discussions on a specific issue, draft clauses, and formally announce them. Individual experts in the country will be asked to conduct individual research to provide reference for the drafting committee, in order to collect opinions widely. Only in this way can it be in line with national conditions, because in the past, the constitutions promulgated in our country did not meet the needs of the people and only copied others, resulting in criticism of closing the door and building a cart. Other matters such as the collection of materials and the investigation of public sentiment have already begun. After the talk will be held next week to allocate work, it will begin immediately.

Head of State System 83

(Question) During the constitutional period, will the head of state of the government adopt a presidential system or a committee system? (Answer) According to Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Founding Program, it is clearly stipulated as a presidential system. In fact, the title of the head of state, whether president or chairman, is acceptable. The important point lies in the provisions of the powers. However, the current organization of the National Government is a committee system. Analyzing its meaning, it should obviously bear the weight of the country's entire administration, but at the same time, the Executive Yuan is responsible to another meeting organization outside the National Government, which forms what is generally called a responsible cabinet system. Then the National Government has nothing to do. In my opinion, the system of our country's political organization does not have to be the same as that of European and American countries, because the National Government is based on five places standing side by side, and the central hub of politics is concentrated in the Central Political Conference. If the Executive Yuan is a responsible cabinet, and the other four Yuans, the Legislative, Judicial, Examination, and Control Yuans, are equally obedient to the Central Political Conference, then what will its name mean? Therefore, the provisions regarding the powers of the head of state in the future should not go beyond two paths: (1) The head of state concurrently serves as the head of the executive branch; (2) The head of state only bears the name of representing the country internally and externally, but does not bear the responsibility of administration. Which way to go still needs to be discussed before a decision can be made.

Referendum Authority 84

(Question) The referendum is one of the direct democratic rights and is extremely important for the quality of politics. However, how should it be stipulated to be in line with our country's national conditions? (Answer) The scope of the referendum on ordinary laws is strictly restricted in European and American countries, to the extent that the people have no way to exercise it. If so, it is tantamount to剥削 the people's due rights and abilities. Looking at Germany's experience, the people mostly lack interest in the referendum. If the scope of the referendum is expanded as much as possible, and everything is changed, it will only delay things more, and the decision of policies will be hindered. The first drawback is that the people, feeling the complexity of the referendum, will tend to give up voting willingly. If so, how can the problem be solved? The second drawback is that our country's current level of education is still young, local autonomy has not yet been fully realized, the population lacks accurate statistics, and the strength of the security forces is weak, all of which are enough to affect the implementation of the referendum. Other matters such as elections, recall, and initiative also suffer from the same difficulties. Looking back at our country's past election results is enough to see the future. The only remedy is for the government to vigorously promote education and promote local autonomy. Only then can it be effective.

Land Issue 85

(Question) How will the land policy be stipulated in the future? (Answer) The purpose of the state's land consolidation is to make the best use of the land and to enable the people to have the right to enjoy and use the land equally. The essence of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's advocacy of equalization of land ownership lies in this. To achieve this advocacy, it is necessary to prevent private monopolies of land in order to seek improper gains, and it is also necessary to find ways to make the increase in the value of the land itself, which is not obtained as a result of capital and labor improvements, be owned by the public. In order to achieve this goal, the most effective means is to levy taxes according to land value and to collect land appreciation tax. The main points are: (1) Land tax is levied based on value; (2) Land tax adopts a progressive approach; (3) A progressive tax is levied on unearned land appreciation; (4) Light taxes on land improvements; (5) Government's method of acquiring private land; (6) Tax-exempt land; (7) Promote land improvement by increasing land tax or estimating high land value; however, the Land Law was promulgated by the central government long ago. The second important task is to wait for the completion of the Land Implementation Law. In the draft constitution, only the outline can be listed.

Accommodating Political Parties 86

(Question) In the future, what will be the scope of accommodating political parties? (Answer) Accommodating political parties is the advocacy of the general public outside the party, and I also agree with this proposal. In order to improve the country's politics, the central government is also very willing to allow the existence of other political parties, but on the principle of not opposing the Three Principles of the People, because our country is building the country based on the Three Principles of the People. If it violates the Three Principles of the People, it is tantamount to violating the essentials of nation-building. Some say that since there are several political parties with different doctrines in European and American countries, and the state allows them to exist at the same time, why does our country have to be unique? However, the national conditions of various countries are obviously different. Given China's current backwardness in education, economy, construction, transportation, and various other aspects, it is already difficult to promote governance even if the entire nation stands on the same political ideological line. If many diametrically opposed political views suddenly appear, I am afraid that the harm will be tasted before the benefit is seen. It is no different from forcing an infant who is still in swaddling clothes to run, and it is unlikely that he will not fall.

Scope of Amendments 87

(Question) After the draft constitution is completed, should the scope of amendments to the draft constitution be stipulated in advance when the National Assembly is convened? (Answer) This point should be determined according to whether there is a need for future facts. (Question) Should the current Yuans and ministries be established under the separation of five powers? (Answer) Opinions on this issue vary. However, the state's establishment of officials and implementation of policies should first be based on setting up people according to the needs of the matter. Whether there is a need to change the current system in the future should be based on public opinion. Finally, the reporter asked Mr. Zhang Zhiben about his advocacy of drafting the constitution at Tianping Mountain, and asked Mr. Sun what his opinion was. Mr. Sun replied that Mr. Zhang's intention was good, but the members of the Constitutional Drafting Committee themselves have other responsibilities. If all the members leave the capital at the same time, it will have an impact on the Yuan's affairs alone. This refers to the facts. (Riri News Agency)

The Current Situation and Crisis in Kang and Tibet After the Sichuan War 88

Liu Wenhui Unable to Focus Westward

The Dalai Lama Seizes the Opportunity to Eye Kang

Chengdu Correspondence: The long-standing Kang-Tibet dispute has remained unresolved due to repeated delays by the authorities. Last year, Tibetan troops retreated temporarily to avoid attacks by Liu Wenhui's army, intending to regroup in the future to realize their aspiration of unifying Kang and Tibet. Those unaware of the true situation in Kang and Tibet mistakenly believed that the Tibetans would not dare to invade again. In reality, if the Tibetan army finds an opportunity, it will still launch large-scale military operations. A visitor from Xikang spoke of the recent situation on the Kang-Tibet border and the critical crisis. This is recorded below to inform the nation:

"Since the outbreak of the Kang-Tibet war last year, Xikang Province has had a troop strength of three brigades. The main force is concentrated in Dege (originally occupied by Tibetan troops, but recovered after the war) and confronts the Tibetan forces across the Jinsha River. There have been no conflicts between the two sides. Subsequently, the Sichuan war broke out, and Liu Wenhui had no time to focus on Xikang, so he transferred a large part of the troops back to Sichuan to participate in the war. As a result, the defense of Xikang is extremely weak and there is a danger of being attacked by the Tibetan army at any time. The reasons why this has not turned into a major incident are: Firstly, an internal strife once occurred in Lhasa, the capital of Tibet, and the Dalai Lama was driven away by the opposition. At this time, there was also talk of the British sending troops into Tibet to suppress the opposition. Seeing this situation, the opposition was deeply afraid that the British would send troops to invade Tibet and eliminate their forces (the Tibetan monastic class opposed to the Dalai Lama, especially against the British). Therefore, they made concessions to the Dalai Lama. Soon, the Dalai Lama safely returned to Lhasa to preside over political and religious affairs. As a result, he was unable to manage Xikang. This is a major reason why the border defense of Xikang can be temporarily safe. Secondly, the weather in Xikang turned cold, and the snow accumulated more than a foot deep, making it difficult for marching. At the same time, the Qinghai army under Ma Bufang also assisted the Sichuan-Kang army in defending against Tibet, so they can live in peace. Although there are small conflicts on the Jinsha River, it is difficult to form a war situation. This is another reason for the safety of the Xikang border defense. However, the current trend is that the Tibetan army is already preparing for a large-scale invasion. At the same time, the political situation in Xikang is also extremely chaotic, so the western border defense is in a dangerous state. According to reliable sources, there are currently no more than one brigade of Sichuan troops in Xikang. Deng Xiang, the commander of the Second Brigade of the First Division of the Sichuan-Kang Border Defense Army, has now left Dege. A small number of troops at the front have deserted mostly because they cannot endure the cold and hardship. If the Tibetan army invades again, there will be no ability to resist. As for the defense of southern Kang, it is maintained by the Fourth Regiment and Second Battalion under Ma Chenglong in Ba'an County. Kangding, the capital district of Xikang, has long been in a state of anarchy since the Political Affairs Committee was abolished. Now, the military and political affairs of Xikang are entirely presided over by Brigadier General Deng Xiang alone. Deng is originally a soldier and does not understand politics. Recently, he also feels exhausted. The soldiers are full of complaints because they cannot get paid. They are also extremely negligent in defense. Recently, due to the results of the Sichuan war, Liu Wenhui has no ability to focus westward. As a result, rumors are rampant in Kangding. At one moment, it is rumored that Liu Wenhui will retreat to Xikang in defeat. At another moment, it is rumored that the Tibetan troops will take the opportunity to launch a large-scale invasion. Seeing this situation, Deng Xiang specifically announced martial law in Kangding and appointed Zhang Zhenzhong, the commander of the Fortieth Regiment, as the commander of the Kangding city defense, responsible for maintaining security in Kangding. The regiment was originally stationed in the front of Dege, but has now been secretly transferred back to rehearse its empty city plan to intimidate the Tibetans. Unfortunately, the Tibetan side discovered it. It is heard that the key pass of Qamdo (Xikang) is now occupied by the Tibetan army as a place to station troops to spy on Kang.) The Tibetan soldiers are eager to try and are consulting the Dalai Lama. Therefore, the future of the Kang border is cause for concern."

Wu Zhongxin Returns to Anhui to Resume His Duties 89

Organizing the Finances and Security Forces of Various Counties

Anqing Correspondence: Wu Zhongxin, the Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, felt that the finances were difficult and his work was constrained. Therefore, at the end of last year, he took the opportunity to attend the Third Plenary Session in Beijing and repeatedly resigned to the Central Government. He lingered in Suzhou and Shanghai, unwilling to return to his post. Recently, the Central Government, feeling that the national crisis was becoming more urgent, exhorted him with righteousness and promised that the Ministry of Finance would allocate 100,000 yuan per month from the aid funds to Anhui Province. Wu then returned to the province on the Qingpu ship at 4 pm on the 31st of last month, accompanied by Ye Yuanlong, the Director of Finance, Liu Yiyan, the Director of Construction, and secretaries Mei Guangyu and Zeng Xiaolu, and resumed his duties on the same day. Luo Liangjian, the Director of Civil Affairs, and Zhang Dingxun, the Provincial Committee Member and Director of Security, will also return soon. According to Wu, the things he intends to actively carry out in the near future are: 1. Cleaning up the local finances of various counties; 2. Reorganizing the security forces of various counties; 3. Opening up roads in the provincial capital. Detailed measures for each of these items are currently being drafted. In order to assess the administrative performance of various counties, the Department of Civil Affairs issued administrative report forms and instructions in June of last year, ordering each county to compile detailed reports from July of last year and submit them to the Provincial Government and the Department of Civil Affairs for review within five days after the end of each month. However, most counties failed to comply and submit the reports, making it impossible to conduct assessments. Therefore, the counties have been telegraphed again, requiring them to fill in and submit monthly administrative reports from January of this year, detailing the important policies related to reforms carried out during the month, the progress of handling them, the current stage of progress, the implementation of new laws and regulations, and various matters such as bandit suppression and rural cleansing, in accordance with the original forms, and submit them by the end of the fifth day of each month for assessment. (February 2)

The Declining Social Scene in Fuzhou 90

Many Small and Medium-Sized Stores Have Closed Down

Refugees from Northern Fujian Still Have No Relief Measures

Fuzhou Correspondence: Fujian's commerce was extremely depressed last year due to the impact of the current situation. Exports such as tea, wood, paper, and bamboo shoots have been completely halted due to the increasingly dangerous situation in the north. Imports such as silk fabrics from Jiangsu and Guangdong are also sluggish due to the changing situation in the province and the sudden increase in unemployment. Businesses are unable to turn over capital and are flocking to banks and money shops to withdraw funds for emergency relief. Seeing this situation, the banking and money industries are also holding firm and tightening credit. For shops that are not very solid, they are cutting off loans to those whose current account books cannot be cleared on time. Even for reliable shops, the amount of loans is greatly reduced. Therefore, the amount of checks for receipts and payments in the market has recently been no more than five or six hundred yuan at most, and it is rare to see two or three thousand yuan. As credit becomes tighter, the number of bankruptcies increased greatly during the Lunar New Year settlement period. However, most of those that went bankrupt were small and medium-sized stores. Few bankruptcies amounted to more than ten thousand yuan. Because the smaller the business, the narrower the scope of activity. Whenever money shops cut off loans, there is no other way but to declare bankruptcy. On the social front, because money shops are mostly unable to recover the loans they have made, their coffers are necessarily empty. If a store's reputation is slightly bad, there are rumors that it will become unstable. On Lunar New Year's Eve, the two branches of the Southeast Bank in Chengtan simultaneously experienced bank runs, and the situation was extremely turbulent. Fortunately, peer banks such as Huainan, Fufeng, and Yi Yuan provided strong assistance, which helped them overcome the difficulties. By late evening, the situation gradually subsided. It was found that the bank was opened by the naval community and issued about one million yuan in banknotes. About 500,000 yuan were circulating in northern Fujian, and the rest were scattered in the Fuzhou market. On that day, the salaries issued by the military and political circles mostly used the bank's banknotes, and those circulating in northern Fujian were returned to Fuzhou for settlement, causing the Southeast Bank's banknotes to suddenly become crowded in the market, causing social misunderstandings. As for pawnshops, after political figures became unemployed, many resorted to pawning goods for a living. There were more pawnings than redemptions, and capital was limited, making it impossible to turn over capital. Therefore, two measures were discussed and decided: one was to shorten business hours, opening for only four hours in the morning and closing in the afternoon; the other was to limit the amount of pawns, with a maximum price of only ten yuan for any item. As a result, the lives of ordinary people became even more difficult. However, the most suffering were the refugees from Chong'an and Guangze counties in northern Fujian who fled the red disaster to the province last autumn, numbering about several hundred. They lived in various temples and guild halls, and the government has not yet provided any relief measures. They are entirely dependent on various charitable organizations and philanthropists to provide food on a rotating basis. Now, due to the long duration of the disaster, their strength is exhausted, and they have also stopped providing relief. These refugees have fallen into a state of hunger and cold. Although representatives have run around and appealed, no one has responded, and they will soon become ghosts in a foreign land.

Hebei Agricultural Report 91

Preliminary Estimates of Main Crop Harvests

Department of Agricultural Economics, Jinling University

In order to help people understand the agricultural situation in the country, the Department of Agricultural Economics of Jinling University's College of Agriculture has been conducting a national agricultural situation survey and assessment on a trial basis since January 1932. This survey includes the harvest and yield of major agricultural products in each province and the facts about the prosperity and decline of the rural economy in various regions. On January 1 of this year, preliminary estimates of the harvest of major crops in Jiangsu Province were published. Now, based on 345 reports from 99 counties in Hebei Province, preliminary estimates of the harvest of major crops in Hebei Province are made as follows:

Table 1: Harvest Quantities of Major Crops in Hebei Province Each Year (Quantities are in units of 10,000 dan, each dan equals 100 jin)

| Main Crop Name | Quantity Harvested in a Year of Abundant Harvest | Average Annual Harvest Quantity in the Last 5-6 Years | Harvest Quantity in 1931 | Harvest Quantity in 1932 |

| ------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------- | ---------------------- |

| Crops Sown in Autumn and Winter, Harvested in Spring and Summer | | | | |

| Wheat | 5,498 | 3,069 | 3,146 | 2,995 |

| Barley | 805 | 483 | 485 | 473 |

| Crops Sown in Spring and Summer, Harvested in Autumn and Winter | | | | |

| Sorghum | 4,048 | 2,545 | 2,710 | 2,851 |

| Millet | 5,037 | 3,312 | 3,365 | 3,228 |

| Broomcorn Millet | 38 | 21 | 22 | 19 |

| Corn | 3,088 | 2,056 | 2,077 | 2,099 |

| Soybeans | 1,943 | 1,123 | 1,128 | 1,122 |

| Sweet Potatoes | 1,965 | 1,507 | 1,394 | 1,549 |

| Cotton | 343 | 225 | 237 | 187 |

| Peanuts | 937 | 633 | 659 | 736 |

Note: The quantities in the table are calculated based on the harvest yield and usual planting area of each year.

Comparing the numbers listed in the table, we can see the amount of harvest each year.

Table 2: Percentage of Harvest Quantity of Major Crops in Hebei Province in 1932 to Harvest Quantity of Each Year (The harvest quantity of each year is 100%)

| Main Crop Name | Percentage of Abundant Harvest | Percentage of Average Harvest in the Last 5-6 Years | Percentage of Harvest in 1931 |

| ------------- | -------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------- | ------------------------ |

| Wheat | 54 | 98 | 95 |

| Barley | 59 | 98 | 98 |

| Sorghum | 70 | 112 | 105 |

| Millet | 64 | 96 | 96 |

| Broomcorn Millet | 49 | 90 | 86 |

| Corn | 68 | 102 | 101 |

| Soybeans | 58 | 100 | 99 |

| Sweet Potatoes | 79 | 119 | 111 |

| Cotton | 55 | 83 | 79 |

| Peanuts | 79 | 116 | 111 |

According to the above table, the summer crops in 1932 were less than 60% of the harvest in abundant years, slightly lower than the harvest in 1921 and the last 5-6 years. Among the autumn crops, sweet potatoes and peanuts had the best harvest, about 80% of the harvest in abundant years, 10% more than in 1931, and more than 15% more than in the last 5-6 years. Sorghum and corn were about 70% of the harvest in abundant years, similar to the harvest in 1931 and the last 5-6 years. Millet is the most important crop in Hebei Province, but the harvest was only 64% of the harvest in abundant years, 4% less than in 1931 and normal years. The harvest of cotton was less than 60% of the harvest in abundant years, also 20% less than in 1931 and normal years.

Table 3: Percentage of Harvest Quantity of Major Crops in Hebei Province Each Year to Harvest Quantity in Abundant Years (The harvest quantity in abundant years is 100%)

| Main Crop Name | Percentage of Average Harvest in the Last 5-6 Years | Percentage of Harvest in 1931 | Percentage of Harvest in 1932 |

| ------------- | ---------------------------------------------- | ------------------------ | ------------------------ |

| Wheat | 56 | 57 | 54 |

| Barley | 60 | 60 | 59 |

| Sorghum | 63 | 67 | 70 |

| Millet | 66 | 67 | 64 |

| Broomcorn Millet | 54 | 56 | 49 |

| Corn | 67 | 67 | 68 |

| Soybeans | 58 | 58 | 58 |

| Sweet Potatoes | 77 | 71 | 79 |

| Cotton | 66 | 69 | 55 |

| Peanuts | 68 | 70 | 79 |

The most important crops in Hebei Province are wheat, sorghum, millet, corn, and cotton. According to the above table, the harvest of wheat in normal years, the previous year, and last year was similar, about 55% of the harvest in abundant years. Sorghum, millet, and corn were about 65% of the harvest in abundant years in normal years, and roughly equal in the previous year and last year, about 67-68% of the harvest. Cotton was about 65% of the harvest in abundant years in normal years, about 70% in the previous year, and only 55% last year.

The above is the situation of provincial statistics, but the counties in Tianjin, Hebei, and the Northeast had 80% harvest in both summer and autumn last year, even cotton had 70% harvest, which was more abundant than the previous year and even more abundant than normal years. (February 1)

County Court Changed to District Court 93

Lin Biao, President of the Jiangsu High Court, convened a meeting of the High Court's division chiefs, judges, and prosecutors on the 3rd to prepare for the implementation of the three-level, three-instance system based on the Court Organization Law promulgated by the Ministry of Justice. It was decided to establish the Tongshan High Court Fourth Branch and set up a District Court. The county courts established in the past will be uniformly changed to District Courts. In addition, due to the large number of civil and criminal cases in the second instance of this court, it was decided to add one civil and one criminal division each. All funding issues will be referred to Minister Luo by President Lin in Beijing for instructions. The above resolutions will be implemented uniformly within this month.

Zhenjiang

Rectifying Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Long-Distance Buses 97

Zhou Hengmou, a chief clerk from the Secretariat of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Luo Huili, a chief clerk from the Construction Department, were previously ordered to inspect the Sheng'an levee. After completing their official duties, they took the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou long-distance bus back to Zhenjiang. Unexpectedly, the bus overturned for no reason on a flat road with no obstacles, less than a mile from the Yangzhou station, causing minor injuries to the two chief clerks and all passengers. The clerks requested the Provincial Government to order the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou bus company to be punished for the driver's carelessness, the overturning of the bus for no reason, and the ticket inspector's failure to stop the illegal act of overloading passengers. After receiving the report, the Provincial Government ordered the Construction Department to instruct Ma Zhenbang, the County Magistrate of Jiangdu County, to warn the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Automobile Company and issue four types of banning rules to prevent such incidents. The rules are as follows: 1. The company's vehicles must be inspected in accordance with the regulations. Vehicles that fail the inspection shall not be allowed to operate. 2. In accordance with the revised "Temporary Regulations for Automobile Donations in Jiangsu Province", the number of people in each vehicle shall be subject to quarterly donations and shall not be overloaded. 3. The company's drivers shall uniformly comply with the banning rules of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department. 4. The efficiency of automobile driving is stipulated to be no more than 25 miles per hour.

Cancellation of Fisheries Office 98

The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously received a report from the former Department of Industry, which was forwarded by the Songjiang County Government, requesting that the Fisheries Administration's Songjin Feng Office be stopped from ordering fishermen to pay fees and obtain licenses in the inland rivers. The government consulted the Ministry of Industry, which instructed it to stop the practice. The Ministry of Industry replied that all fisheries offices and fish protection teams have been abolished. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has now ordered the two departments of Civil Affairs and Construction to be notified.

Except for Huang Xiaolao Wang and Tang Lunxue, who escaped, the remaining 78 were pursued and captured in separate groups and killed on the spot.

Shi Zhaoda of Yizhuang, 12th District, Yiyi, led a group of accomplices to rob Wu Jinliang's house in Hefengwei, 10th District, last November, injuring the victim. He was interrogated strictly, and Wu Bosheng, the victim, and Xu Jixiang, the witness, were summoned to court to prove everything. Shi Confessed to the murder. A death sentence was decreed to be issued to Shi Zhaoda who was immediately signed on the previous day by the county government following the provincial telegraph, bound to the western suburbs and shot, and announced.

Hangzhou

Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Improves Salt Transportation 106

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau has been implementing salt transportation in Yu Dai, eastern Zhejiang, which is a salt-producing area. In order to improve salt transportation, it has formulated improvements and will be implemented from February 1: 1. Regarding the preparation of vehicles for salt, the railway bureau has increased the number of vehicles, and the Linpu station can reserve empty vehicles in the future, so there is no need to worry about shortages. 2. Regarding the preparation of good vehicles, the railway bureau has newly purchased 15-ton vehicles, and there will be no problem in using 15 tons. 3. Regarding the postponement of salt loading and unloading during rainy days, the loading and unloading time can be extended in accordance with the regulations during heavy rains. 4. The original boatmen shall be limited to transporting salt outside the loading and unloading area.

Page 13

Local News

Wu Chaoshu Talks About Domestic and Foreign Affairs 108

Council of State to be Convened Within the Year

Little Hope for League of Nations' Recommendations

Southwest Decides to Cooperate with the Central Government

Wu Chaoshu, a member of the Central Committee, went to Beijing to attend the drafting committee of the Organizational Regulations of the National Council of State. Yesterday morning at 8 o'clock, he returned to Shanghai from Beijing by night express train. A reporter from this newspaper visited Wu at his residence yesterday and was granted an audience. Wu spoke in detail about the National Council of State, the Rehe issue, and the recent international situation. He also said that he had expressed his determination to the Central Government not to take up the position of Minister of Justice. His remarks are divided as follows:

National Council of State 109

Wu first said that the drafting committee of the Organizational Regulations of the National Council of State was appointed by the Central Political Council and is dedicated to discussing the method of producing the National Council of State and all organizational laws and regulations. It is now scheduled to hold a meeting once a week, and I will also go to Beijing to attend at any time. It is expected that all work will be completed in one or two months. Then, it will be handed over to the Central Political Council to the Legislative Yuan, which will formulate various laws and regulations based on the principles agreed upon by this committee. As for the convocation period, in any case, it will be within this year.

Our Advantage Lies in Perseverance 110

Wu also said that the Japanese army's attack on Rehe is a foregone conclusion. Our country also has considerable preparations. In any case, we must do our best to contend with the enemy, so that the enemy must pay twelve points in return to obtain even an inch of our land. From a military point of view, our advantage lies in perseverance, and the enemy's advantage lies in a quick battle. Therefore, temporary victories or defeats are not worth paying attention to. There must be a real long-term resistance. The enemy will be exhausted, and the domestic economy will tend to collapse due to military consumption. Once the weakness is broken, the final victory will belong to us.

Only Two Miles a Day 111

Wu then cited a very wonderful analogy: In the Battle of Shanghai, the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army bravely resisted the Japanese for more than 30 days before calmly retreating to the second line of defense. The Japanese army's expansion was limited to Nanxiang. From Shanghai to Wusong to Nanxiang, it was about 60 Chinese miles, that is, only two miles were lost per day. The Japanese army gained only 60 miles at such a heavy sacrifice. I hope that the Rehe defending army will not let the 19th Route Army and others monopolize the beauty of the past.

English Mediation 112

The reporter inquired about the widely rumored mediation by British Ambassador Lampson, and the proposed buffer zone neutral territory, etc. Mr. Wu said he had not heard of them, only stating that since the British Foreign Office had formally denied siding with Japan and the existence of a secret Anglo-Japanese agreement, there would be no further obvious actions. The League of Nations' Committee of Nineteen's recommendation report is about to be completed, and we should wait and see the facts. However, I deeply believe that no matter what, it will definitely not harm Japan or force Japan to obey. The maximum our country can obtain is only the sympathy of international moral opinion. I have never had extravagant hopes for the League of Nations from the beginning, so the result today is not disappointing.

Southwest Decides to Cooperate 113

Regarding the Southwest, there have been various rumors of provocations by the Japanese. Mr. Wu said that as far as he knows, if the central government is determined to resist, the Southwest will cooperate with the central government. As for my position as Minister of Justice and Administration, I have already expressed my firm intention to the central government not to take it. Finally, regarding the incident of Gu Zhutong illegally shooting journalist Liu Yusheng, Mr. Wu stated that even in the late Qing Dynasty, when political darkness reached its peak, officials still did not dare to treat human life lightly. Prisoners awaiting trial had to wait for the Qing Emperor's endorsement before being executed in the autumn assizes. Today, even company commanders and platoon leaders can casually put people to death. His words were filled with emotion.

Sun Ke Discusses Issues Such as Political Participation and Constitutionalism 114

The powers of the Political Participation Council and the Legislative Yuan do not conflict.

Drafting of the constitution is in active preparation.

Central News Agency reports: Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai the night before last from Nanjing with Legislative Yuan members Ma Chaojun, Jian Youwen, Zhong Tianxin, Chen Jianru, and others. A Central News Agency reporter visited them yesterday morning, and the following is a record of their conversations:

National Political Participation 115

The drafting committee of the organizational regulations for the National Political Participation Council held its first meeting in Nanjing on the 2nd, where they discussed in detail issues such as the number of members, method of selection, powers, and term of office. However, no concrete decisions have been made and further discussions are needed. The National Political Participation Council is a public opinion organ during the period of political tutelage, which summarizes national public opinion and presents it to the government, serving as a transitional mechanism from political tutelage to constitutionalism. In other words, it is the "ladder" for entering the constitutional period. Therefore, its central task is not "legislation" but "recommendation", which is different from the Legislative Yuan's task of "legislation". Rumors that the establishment of the National Political Participation Council will lead to conflicts with the Legislative Yuan in terms of powers are based on a misunderstanding of the nature of the two. As for the selection and number of members of the National Political Participation Council, a small number will be appointed by the central government, and the majority will be elected, so that it becomes a public opinion organ worthy of the name. Due to the fact that local autonomy in various provinces has not been fully implemented, general elections are difficult to carry out, and a group election method will be adopted. All parties do not advocate for too many members, but a number greater than the number of legislators is acceptable.

Legislative Work 116

The drafting of the constitution is in active preparation, and the first meeting of the draft committee has been scheduled for the 9th of this month to discuss methods of grouping and soliciting opinions on the draft constitution from all walks of life. The revision of current civil and criminal laws and regulations is also under consideration. I believe that in the past, the drafting of various laws and regulations was often done by a few people based on subjective opinions, which was almost like building a car behind closed doors. Laws and regulations of this kind of "paperwork" naturally cannot fully conform to the national sentiment, and foreignized laws and regulations drafted solely based on foreign laws and regulations are even less suitable for our country's situation. The Legislative Yuan should eliminate this drawback in the future. Whenever a law is enacted, a general outline must first be drafted, distributed to various places, and solicit opinions from all localities as much as possible for reference. Such legislation can be suitable for local conditions, because legislation should emphasize public sentiment, not just legal principles.

Reorganizing Laws and Regulations 117

The Central Political Council has resolved to establish an Administrative Regulations Reorganization Committee, because it recognizes that the organizations of various agencies under the National Government are complex, and the laws and regulations are inconsistent, which causes great inconvenience in administration. Therefore, it is now actively planning to complete the reorganization work within one year. The chairman is concurrently held by Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan.

The League of Nations is Powerless 118

Japan has long had the idea of withdrawing from the League of Nations, perhaps because the League of Nations has not been able to completely prevent its invasion of China. In our country, recently, due to the weakness and powerlessness of the League of Nations, which has been unable to solve the Northeast problem for more than a year, some people advocate withdrawing from the League of Nations. This is because they believe that the League of Nations cannot speak out for justice and implement its covenants. In order to maintain the credibility of the League of Nations and maintain world peace, it can resolutely withdraw when necessary. Britain and France are the pillars of the League of Nations. We hope that the governments of both countries will respect international charters and take concrete actions. Britain has now stated that it is prepared to base its actions on the Lytton Report. What the result will be remains to be seen.

Southwest National Defense 119

Due to the geographical relationship, the southwestern provinces have close ties in terms of defense. It is now heard that there is also an organization of the Southwest National Defense Committee, but it can only be formally established after the central government approves it. The central government also has a proposed National Defense Committee. In the future, the Southwest National Defense Committee can be subordinate to the Central National Defense Committee.

Other Issues 120

Sun Ke believes that the case of the Jiangsu Provincial Government shooting Liu Yusheng was a major mistake. Sun continued by saying that with regard to the southward relocation of cultural relics from Beiping, land and people are ultimately more important than cultural relics, so it does not seem appropriate to relocate cultural relics urgently. Sun said that because he had to attend the preparatory meeting of the Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Institute, he would return to Nanjing around Tuesday or Wednesday.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Telegram to Encourage Tang Yulin 121

Only you can be relied on to keep the country intact.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed Chairman Tang in Chengde yesterday, saying that since the Japanese army is about to launch a large-scale attack on Rehe again: "Chairman Tang of Chengde, Xunjian, I received the telegram on Jianri, and I also saw Chief Cui's report from Kailu, a colorful telegram rejecting the enemy. It shows your sincerity in defending the country and the unity of the soldiers. I deeply admire you. All sectors of the city have recently organized a consolation association. We will do our best to raise donations for the supplies needed on the front line to serve as a backing. With a strong enemy in front of us and the war just beginning, I still hope that you will consult with Director Zhang in Beiping to actively plan for defense. Only you can be relied on to keep the country intact." Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Various Sectors Actively Raise Funds to Purchase Airplanes

Raising Funds for the "National Goods" Aircraft 122

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods, at its first dinner party for the National Goods Year, Chen Binghui proposed that the four national goods organizations should jointly raise funds for the "National Goods" aircraft to save the country. Yang Xingfo's Talk 125

The Mission and Impressions of Going to Beiping

Yang Xingfo, Director-General of the Academia Sinica, returned to Shanghai from Beiping yesterday. The reporter specially visited him to inquire about his mission and impressions of going to Beiping. The questions and answers are recorded as follows: (Question) There are different rumors about your mission to Beiping this time. What is it? (Answer) I went to Beiping this time to inspect the work of the Institute of History and Language and the Institute of Psychology of the Academia Sinica in Beiping, and to discuss the progress plans of the two institutes. At the same time, I took the opportunity to assist Mr. Li Ji and Hu Shi in organizing the Beiping Branch of the China League for the Protection of Civil Rights, and entrusted by a friend to deliver a letter to the China Women's Relief and Comfort Association in Beiping, and to investigate the organization and equipment of the Northern Relief and Anti-Japanese Wounded Soldiers. This trip does not represent any individual. I made a solemn statement in the Women's Relief and Comfort Association. (Question) I heard that you inspected the wounded soldier hospitals and various prisons. What did you see? (Answer) The only place in Beiping that now houses wounded soldiers is the Weishu Hospital, which has 600 wounded soldiers, about one-third of whom were injured in Yuguan by the Ninth Brigade. The hospital was converted from a factory, and the monthly funding is only three to four thousand yuan, so the equipment is very simple. In addition, there is a temporary relief hospital that is still being prepared, located in the old barracks of the Shifuyuan, which is larger in area and can accommodate 2,000 beds, and is managed by the Beiping Municipal Government. Recently, no new wounded soldiers have been sent from the Yuguan area. It is heard that the most needed for relief are in the Rehe area, but the climate there is extremely cold and the transportation is very inconvenient, and adequate preparations must be made before it can be dealt with. As for the inspection of prisons, it was because the Beiping Branch of the China League for the Protection of Civil Rights elected me, Mr. Hu Shi, and Cheng Ping to visit political prisoners detained in Beiping. The places we went to were the Army Prison Military Branch, the Repentance Institute, and the Detention Center of the Military Law Enforcement Office. There are about 30 political prisoners in the Army Prison, and all 92 people in the Repentance Institute are political prisoners. There are more than 20 political prisoners in the Detention Center of the Military Law Enforcement Office. In recent months, some of the students arrested by the Anti-Japanese Association have been convicted and entered the Repentance Institute, and some are still in the detention center. All the prisoners in the above three places wear extremely heavy fetters. Their detention is based on the Emergency Punishment Law for Endangering the Republic of China and has not been formally tried in court. (Question) What is the situation of the southward relocation of cultural relics in Beiping? (Answer) More than 3,000 boxes of cultural relics from the Palace Museum in Beiping have been packed, but due to the difficulty of vehicles and the laziness of the laborers, they have not yet been loaded when I left. As for the 120 boxes that were rumored to have arrived in Shanghai, they are fragments of excavated cultural relics, rubbings, and books and instruments for research by the two institutes of the Academia Sinica in Beiping, because a part of the two institutes has been decided by the institute to move south.

The Water Fee Problem is Becoming Increasingly Complex 130

The company uses water cut-offs as a means of increasing fees.

Users use water tapping as a means of self-defense.

||| Real Estate Sector's Emergency Meeting Tomorrow |||

The water fee problem in the Public Concession, in the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930), due to the fluctuating gold and silver exchange rates, the British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company requested and was approved by the Public Works Department to add a surcharge of one-fourth. For a time, people rose up in opposition, and water cut-offs and non-payment turned into a huge storm. Fortunately, the Public Works Department handled it appropriately, and the first stage came to an end. Last year, the water company, based on a report by Hill's experts, believed that controlling the waste of tap water was the only solution and proposed the widespread installation of water meters to calculate water fees. After being approved by the Public Works Department and installing the meters, the waste was not controlled, and the water meters were several times higher than the rent when calculated based on the rent. In some cases, it even exceeded the rent. The landlords who paid the water fees then requested the Shanghai Real Estate Association to negotiate, but it was not resolved. After several months of delay, someone mediated and invited representatives from the Public Works Department, the water company, and the Real Estate Association to exchange views. The mediator and the water company and the Real Estate Association each submitted statements for further discussion. At the same time, the landlords were about to decide whether to pay the water fees based on the inclusive water system. However, the water company either completely refused or demanded additional payments, otherwise they would cut off the water. Those whose water was cut off included the Yangshupu, Huasheng Road, Fenzhou Road, Biford, and Bilu industrial properties of Elly & Company. The water company closed the faucets at 11:00 am last December. Next, starting from February 12, the Tangshan Road and Baoding Road of Huada Foreign Company, Fuyuanli, the Zhejiang Road and Niuzhuang Road of Fenxing Company, Weishuifang, the Yangshupu Road and Huaxingfang of the American-owned Yizhong Bank Company, and the Lingqing Road and Qinyuli industrial properties of Qinyu Company all received the same treatment from the water company. The above industrial properties had dozens, hundreds, or even two to three hundred buildings, either in the commercial center or in the workers' area. After the water was cut off, people were greatly frightened, as if a great disaster was about to happen. The landlords, because people cannot live without water for a moment, were forced to implement emergency self-defense under the law and automatically tapped the water to ensure the lives of the residents and maintain public safety. The Shanghai Real Estate Association saw that the situation was becoming increasingly serious. On the one hand, it sent a letter to the Public Works Department and the water company, and on the other hand, it convened an emergency meeting. The association's letters are excerpted below:

Real Estate Sector's ······ Emergency Meeting Tomorrow 131

The Shanghai Real Estate Association yesterday urgently sent a letter to all members saying, "Most urgent: Since the British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company forced the installation of water meters, water fees have skyrocketed, and property owners cannot afford it. Most have paid at the old prices, leaving the rest to be resolved. However, recently, because they were unsuccessful in forcing price increases, they implemented high-pressure tactics, cutting off the water supply. Landlords and tenants alike are suffering and have reported to the association. It has now been decided to convene an emergency meeting of the entire real estate sector at the association's office at 96 Beijing Road at 3:00 pm on Monday, February 6, and representatives of tenants whose water has been cut off are requested to report on the situation. We hope you will attend the meeting at that time and propose solutions as much as possible. We are deeply grateful."

Real Estate Association ··· To the Public Works Department 132

"We would like to inquire about the water price issue, which has been suspended for a long time. The opinions of all parties have been submitted to your bureau for two months, and citizens often inquire with this association about what solutions your bureau has adopted for this matter. Since the waterworks company has been cutting off the water supply during this period, the situation has become more complicated, and it is difficult to conceal the anger of the people. Most of the landlords whose water has been cut off are waiting for the results of the meeting to decide on a solution. Being suddenly subjected to adversity, how can they bear it? Some landlords have even paid according to the old prices out of consideration for the company, but the company has refused to accept it. Within this week, there have been three cases of water cut-offs: 1. The water supply to the Yuanfuli houses on Baoding Road, leased by Huada Foreign Company, was cut off at 2:00 pm on January 30. 2. The water supply to the Huaxinfang houses on Yangshupu Road, leased by Yizhong Company, was cut off at 2:00 pm on January 31. 3. The water supply to the Weishuifang houses on Niuzhuang Road, leased by Fenxing Company, was cut off at 10:00 am on February 2. While mediation is underway and the entire case is being handled by your bureau in order to find a satisfactory solution, the above cases have occurred one after another, which is what this association does not understand. Since the waterworks company has accepted mediation, it should not adopt such extreme measures against users, especially when the amount of water prices to be paid by users is the crux of the problem and urgently needs to be resolved. This kind of action is greatly contrary to local welfare. We believe that your bureau and this association share the same view. Before the entire problem is resolved, it should be stopped immediately. Now your bureau is aware of the opinions accumulated by all parties concerned. Can you please provide details of the solutions you intend to formulate to resolve this case? Prolonging this matter is really useless. We are sending this letter accordingly, and we hope you will investigate it."

Real Estate Association ··· To the Waterworks Company 133

"We would like to inform you that the member Fenxing Company has sent a letter stating that it has received a letter from the British Waterworks Company instructing it to find 153 yuan, 4 jiao, and 5 fen to make up for the water fees before November of last year, and that it must be paid before February 1 of this year, otherwise the water will be cut off. This company acts entirely on justice and fairness and on the ability to abide by legal and moral principles. Therefore, all water fees before November of last year have been paid in accordance with the regulations. If we were to allow people to take whatever they want under duress, how would we protect our legal interests? In short, this company will comply with whatever method is decided by all three parties. Before the three parties decide on a method, except for the water fees that have already been paid in accordance with the inclusive water system, any behavior or changes that are beyond the company's ability cannot be prevented. It is confirmed that this is a commercial relationship, not a relationship between the ruler and the ruled. We are sending this letter accordingly and request that your association forward it to the company for investigation."

Huada Company ···· To the Real Estate Association 134

"We would like to inform you that the hundred houses in Yuanfuli on Tangshan Road of this office, the water company has changed to the water meter system since July, and the water fees have increased sharply, with the maximum increase being more than four times. This office did not pay according to the new rates before the water fee issue was resolved. Yesterday, the water company suddenly sent a letter to each tenant, saying that the owner has not paid the water fees and that they would have to stop the water supply. We are particularly writing to inform you that it is now the end of the year, and if the water is cut off, there will be many disputes. Please ask your association to strongly negotiate with the water company and do not use water cut-offs as a threat to avoid more problems. Enclosed are 26 water cut-off slips issued to tenants. Please accept them."

Real Estate Association ······· Reply to Huada Company 135

"We are replying to your letter of January 25, in which you stated that the water company is using water cut-offs as a threat because it is not successful in calculating water fees by meter, and has issued leaflets to tenants stating, etc. We have noted everything. It is found that this kind of water fee calculated by meter is several times higher than the inclusive water system, and neither the landlord nor the tenant can afford to pay it. If the water company insists on going its own way, seeking its own benefit without regard to the damage to others, we can only let it be. Although we are extremely unwilling to see the situation escalate, we cannot avoid it. Please inform us of any news at any time."

Qinyu Company ···· To the Waterworks Company 136

"We would like to inform you that this company has sent up the water fees twice, originally as a transitional measure, pending the three parties deciding on a new method before following it. However, this sincerity of seeking peace has not been understood by your company, and the checks have been returned twice, which is extremely regrettable. We are even more saddened by the different treatment. This company is in a situation where it is not unwilling, but unable to act. We can only let things develop naturally, but this company cannot bear the responsibility. We are sending this letter accordingly, hoping that you will investigate it."

Letter to the Anti-War League 139

Respected Sirs, the fall of the Northeast shook the whole country. All our countrymen are filled with indignation. In this critical moment of life and death for the nation, Jiang brazenly launched a war, leading troops to Guizhou. We feel deeply ashamed. Our army commander, General Wang, in order to implement the policy of resisting foreign aggression, reorganized his troops and first quelled the internal strife. Fortunately, the war has been pacified and the situation in Guizhou has been stabilized, which is in line with your earnest expectations. Your association's call for peace and your concern for the Guizhou army are deeply appreciated. We hereby attach the latest telegram from General Wang for your review and reassurance. Sincerely yours, The Guizhou Provincial Government and the Twenty-Fifth Army Representatives, Xu Chaoguang and Deng Houfang, respectfully.

There is no base. I, Lie, have sent a special letter to invite him to surrender. If he does not comply, it can be easily resolved. Cuixiu Hall Will Re-calibrate Rice Measures Tomorrow 146

We were granted permission. After deliberation by the industry, it was decided to first send one instrument to your office for calibration and return. The Sausage Industry Association's Dissent Regarding Customs Valuation 147

Yesterday, the Sausage Industry Association held an emergency meeting regarding the customs tax assessment, which overvalued the price of sausages.
