Regulations for Foreigners Purchasing Real Estate and Obtaining Certificates 148

The Shanghai Municipal Government Asks the Central Government for Instructions

According to the Central News Agency, foreign churches often purchase land in the interior in the name of establishing schools or other charitable institutions. Although this land is purchased by foreigners, its ownership cannot be regarded as the same as the land ownership of Chinese citizens. The Central News Agency reporter visited the Land Bureau yesterday to inquire about the bureau's current regulations for foreigners purchasing Chinese land. According to the person in charge of the bureau, foreign churches purchase more Chinese land within the scope of Shanghai than in other places. According to Chinese and foreign treaties, there are regulations allowing such purchases. Moreover, churches purchase land for charitable purposes. Therefore, when the bureau organized the land deeds in previous years, it also issued land practice certificates to the land purchased by churches, but added a "permanent lease" stamp on the certificate to indicate that the sovereignty of the land still belongs to China and cannot be the same as the ownership of land purchased by Chinese citizens. However, this measure is only of a temporary nature. The bureau has previously submitted a request to the municipal government to formulate new regulations for compliance. It is recently heard that the municipal government has forwarded the request to the central government for instructions, and the central government has also submitted it to the Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Ministry of Finance for discussion, so that it can be forwarded for compliance.

Italian Ship Libya to Return Home 149

According to the Zi Lin Bao, the Italian cruiser Libya has been stationed in Shanghai for several years. According to news from the Italian Consulate General yesterday (3rd), it will soon leave Shanghai and return home. A newer type of cruiser and a destroyer will sail from Manila to Shanghai to be stationed. The cruiser is named the Guardo, and the destroyer is named the Le Ban Dou.

Workers in the Dried Goods Industry Appealed Yesterday Due to Layoffs 150

The Social Affairs Bureau Agreed to Convene Mediation Tomorrow

More than 70 dried goods stores in Shanghai, including Shao Wansheng, laid off more than 120 workers during the lunar New Year. The workers were worried about their livelihoods and were in a state of panic.

Appealing to the Party and Government Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, the Dried Goods Industry Union sent representatives Yu Yaoqiu, Huang Jiabang, Gong Yimin, and Shao Wenyu, etc., more than a dozen people in total, carrying a petition to the Municipal Party Headquarters, where they were received by Long Peiyun and Dai Yongchan, two staff members of the Civil Affairs Section. After inquiring about their intentions, they agreed to immediately send personnel to investigate Shao Wansheng and other stores, and to cooperate with the Social Affairs Bureau to handle the mediation issue. The representatives also went to the Social Affairs Bureau to appeal, where they were received by Peng Zhenqiu, a staff member of the Third Section. He believed that the number of workers laid off in the dried goods industry this time was too large, and it would be quite difficult to handle the mediation separately. He agreed to convene representatives from the Industry Association and the Labor Union to the bureau at 1:00 PM (tomorrow) to mediate according to law, and advised the workers to return to the store and wait for a solution. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Mediation Tomorrow In addition to receiving the petition from the labor side, the Municipal Party Headquarters believes that the capital side of the dried goods industry still follows the old customs of the lunar calendar, laying off workers, which is inappropriate. Therefore, Dai Yongchan was immediately sent by the Civil Affairs Section to Shao Wansheng and other stores to persuade the capital side not to drive the workers out of the store before the issue is resolved, and to continue to provide food and lodging. On the side of the Social Affairs Bureau, it was decided to convene representatives from the Dried Goods Industry Association and the Occupational Union, two responsible representatives from each, to the bureau at 1:00 PM tomorrow to wait for mediation, so as to quell the labor unrest.

Novelists

A Young Viennese Traveler and Adventurer Comes to Shanghai 151

Feeling the Difficulty of Making a Living by Writing on a Snowy Night

A Whimsical Proposal from a Friend Actually Led to a Trip Around the World

Now Plans to Ask the Panchen Lama for a Passport to Travel to Tibet

According to the Dami Evening Post, a young Viennese novelist, traveler, and adventurer recently arrived in Shanghai from Beiping. His name is Weiss Flach. On the snowy night of February 14, 1928, he was drinking with three or four friends in a wine shop in Vienna. He felt the difficulty of making a living by writing. A friend jokingly suggested, "Why not ride a bicycle around the world to collect good materials for speeches?" Weiss immediately slapped the table and exclaimed, "Excellent! Excellent! This is truly a brilliant plan! I have made up my mind." So, the next morning, he straddled his bicycle and embarked on a long journey through the snow. In the past five years, he has crossed the highest mountains in Europe, traversed the deepest forests in Asia, and crossed the hottest Sahara Desert in the world. He has traveled 46,000 kilometers on his two-wheeled vehicle. When he arrived in Kanpur, India last year, the bicycle was so worn out that he abandoned it and walked or took trains to Shanghai. During the journey, he saw the portraits of the King and Queen of Sweden, and in Finland and Latvia, he went through many twists and turns to obtain the autobiographies of the presidents of the two countries. In Spanish Morocco, he went deep into the chieftain's courtyard and witnessed the exotic dances of the barbarian concubines. After passing through India to Siam, he got lost in the primeval forests for ten days. The servants he hired fled due to the incessant rain, so he ventured alone through the dangers of poisonous snakes and fierce tigers. Finally, he reached a British-operated mine, and was able to return to the civilized world. He recently traveled from Taiwan to Beiping, wanting to ask the Panchen Lama for a passport to travel to Tibet. He then heard that the Panchen Lama was going to Beijing, so he came to Shanghai and will continue to Nanjing to visit the Panchen Lama, hoping to realize his intention to travel to Tibet.

The Pujiang Daily Ship Caused a Disaster 160

The Ship Was Very Fast and Disregarded Everything

A Coal Ship Sank and a Match Ship Was Also Careless

The following is a report on the incident of a Japanese ship causing a disaster at the mouth of Lujiazui in the Pujiang River, colliding with and sinking a coal ship and drowning a boatman:

Coal Ship Capsized A few days ago, a cargo ship named HakushinMaru, belonging to the Japanese Dalian Steamship Company, came to Shanghai from Tianjin and entered the Pujiang River from Wusong. When it reached the Lujiazui river, the ship took advantage of the fast tide. When driving, the ship disregards the cargo ships in the port. At that time, a civilian ship carrying coal was sailing out of the Pujiang River, facing the Japanese ship. When the Japanese ship approached, the coal ship tried to avoid it, but the Japanese ship was very fast and did not slow down, causing the coal ship to be hit hard, damaging the hull and immediately sinking in the port.

Match Carelessness The force of the Japanese ship's collision was huge. After the coal ship was hit, a small civilian ship transporting matches was also hit by the Japanese ship. The ship was loaded with 900 cases of matches, which fell over due to the impact, causing a fire. The fire was raging for a while, and the matches were even easier to burn. In a short time, 45 cases were destroyed. Fortunately, they tried their best to put out the fire, and were able to put it out with water, avoiding a major disaster. However, part of the hull has been burned.

One Person Drowned After the Japanese ship caused an accident and overturned the coal ship, the boatmen in the ship all fell into the water. Fortunately, nearby small boats and the water patrol police sent boats to rescue them, and the people who fell into the water were rescued, but one boatman had already drowned in the Pujiang River. After the incident occurred, the boatman of the coal ship who was victimized reported the collision to the customs and reported to the cargo owner, preparing to negotiate with the Japanese ship of the Dalian Steamship Company that caused the disaster and seek compensation for various losses.

A Passenger Dies Tragically on a Public Bus 167

At around eight o'clock last night, a public bus near Songpan Road, Yangshupu, identified as No. 15132, was speeding from west to east. Old Man Li Fangxiao Sues the Fochi Pharmaceutical Factory for Defamation 168

The Special District Court Continued Hearing Yesterday Afternoon

Li Fangxiao, a 111-year-old man, is suing Feng Mingzheng, the manager of the Fochi Pharmaceutical Factory, for defamation. The hearing was continued yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM in the Fifth Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Both parties appeared in court as summoned. First, Yuan Jingtang, the defendant's lawyer, stated that the Fochi Factory had obtained the plaintiff's full consent before publishing his name and photograph. He presented a photograph of the plaintiff with Yu Huiguan, the chairman of the factory, and Dr. Li Xingrong, along with seven others, as evidence. He also stated that the plaintiff had attended a dinner party in Jinlingchun with the defendant and the chairman of the factory, during which the plaintiff formally allowed the factory to publish his photograph and name. The judge questioned the witnesses, and their testimonies were consistent. The plaintiff admitted to all the statements made, but denied that he had allowed his photograph to be used for advertising. The judge advised both parties to reconcile, but they were both adamant and unwilling to concede. The court adjourned due to the late hour and scheduled the hearing to continue on the 17th of this month, urging them to continue reconciliation efforts in the meantime.

Suspicions Surrounding a Woman's Tragic Death After Childbirth 169

Her brother insists she was beaten to death by her husband

The judge ordered an autopsy of the body

Xin Zhengshi, a Ningbo woman, aged 27, whose husband, Xin Liyun, worked as a clerk at the Texaco oil depot in Pudong, suffered a miscarriage on the 28th of last month, which led to illness. Her husband sent her to the Ximen Maternity Hospital for treatment, but she returned home for recuperation after a few days. The woman's illness suddenly worsened and she died at home the day before yesterday. The woman's brother, Zheng Zhenglin, believed that his sister did not die of illness, but was beaten and injured to death by her husband, Xin Liyun. Therefore, the day before yesterday, he went to the Xin's home with several companions to argue with him and reported it to the Huishan Police Station, ordering detectives to investigate. They moved the woman's body to the Fielun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, they reported to the First Special District Court and requested Prosecutor Guo Wei to come to the morgue to examine the body and hear the case. According to Zheng Zhenglin's testimony, the deceased was his younger sister, and on the first day of the lunar new year, her husband gave the children two yuan in New Year's money, and his sister asked her husband for New Year's money, but he refused, which led to an argument, and he slapped her face and then beat her with fists and feet, causing serious injuries and leading to death. He heard it from the Fan family, a neighbour of the deceased. According to the testimony of the deceased's husband, Xin Liyun, the deceased was his wife, and she died of illness after a miscarriage on the third day of the lunar new year, and there had been no quarrel or fight with her recently. They had a quarrel once in September last year, and requested an examination. Guo Jun said that the truth could only be revealed after an autopsy was performed on the body, so the court ordered an autopsy and rescheduled the hearing for Tuesday next week.

Further Report on the Case of the Anti-Gambling Operations Department Banning a Gambling Den 170

Fines of over four hundred yuan were transferred to the Northeast Volunteer Army

The Gambling Den Property Has Already Been Sealed and Gambling is Strictly Prohibited

The Songhu Garrison Headquarters, based on a confidential report, new New River Danfeng Road Guanyinge Lane Yunshan Lane No. 16, whether unemployed Shanghai gangsters, secretly opened gambling dens, etc., the authorities said that during the martial law period, hundreds of people gathered every day and all night long to gamble, which was related to local public security, so they sent adjutant Zhang Yusan and others, led a platoon of military police, to arrest them at the address at 9:00 p.m. on the 1st of this month. A large number of gambling and smoking paraphernalia were seized on the spot, and more than 300 male and female criminals were arrested. The situation has been briefly reported in the previous report, and the subsequent situation is recorded as follows.

Sentencing of gamblers: After the secret gambling den was raided, all 300 or so gamblers who were arrested, except for the 23 more important ones, were escorted by military police in trucks to the Longhua Headquarters Detention Center for custody. The rest were temporarily guarded by military police downstairs in the gambling den. Until the afternoon of the 2nd, the Garrison Headquarters sent military law officers to the second floor of the gambling den to interrogate the gamblers separately, or fined them four or five yuan, or beat their palms with military sticks several times, as a warning, and then released them all. A total of more than 410 yuan was collected in fines, and it is planned to transfer the money to the Northeast Volunteer Army. After the case is closed, the punishment will be announced. As for the 23 gamblers detained at the Longhua Headquarters, because the circumstances are more serious, they are still being investigated before they are sentenced.

Seizure of the Gambling Property: The gambling den property was sealed off yesterday by personnel from the Garrison Headquarters. Notices were posted on all front and back doors, strictly prohibiting gambling, so that all merchants and others would be informed.

Not much Money was Seized: The previous report stated that tens of thousands of yuan in illegal money was seized from the gambling den. This was a misrepresentation. According to Adjutant Zhang of the Garrison Headquarters, only 119 yuan in silver dollars, 70 jiao in small silver coins, and 27,290 copper coins were seized at the time, as well as four chartered cars and one pistol. However, according to the gambling den's account books, the daily turnover was only three or four hundred yuan, so there could not have been such a large amount of money.

The French Concession Levies a Classified Business Tax 174

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request for Negotiations

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a report to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the French Concession's proposed levy of a classified business tax, please promptly stop it. On the 3rd of this month, the Wood and Bamboo Industry Association of this city sent a letter stating that the members Fuxing, Wanfeng, Chengda, Tongxing, Shenru, Lida, Lishang, Dali, Changhou, and Dali, and Yu Taimaosheng Yiji and other companies, have been operating in the French Concession for many years. In addition to paying municipal donations (i.e. police donations), they have never paid other taxes. Unexpectedly, in January of this year, they successively received notices from the French police, stating that they must donate the so-called classified business donation, etc. If they donate according to the regulations immediately, otherwise they will be fined. The members believe that this item has never existed in the past years, and it is also found that in the so-called classified business regulations, our industry is classified as bamboo and wood rigid material. All the equipment in the store must be subject to the control of the French authorities' public officials. Before starting business, we must first request a donation certificate and pay a review fee of ten yuan in foreign currency. Whether or not it is approved is still subject to the approval of the Engineering Bureau before we can start business. The various regulations are very harsh and cannot be tolerated by our industry. If we do not negotiate reasonably and try to cancel it, in the future, members will inevitably be unable to operate in the concession, which will endanger the future of business. There is no limit to this, and recently it has been found that there have been several cases of members being forced and punished by the French police. Therefore, we have no choice but to request your association to cancel the negotiations with the French Engineering Bureau in order to maintain business. To maintain the industry's safety, this is a matter of public interest. According to this, it is found that the business tax in this city has not yet been implemented. I don't know what legal basis the Engineering Bureau's so-called classified business donation is based on. Please transfer a letter to the association for legal prevention and clarify and reply to maintain business. According to this, it is found that the tax rate for business tax in this city has long been approved by your government and has been approved for implementation. Later, after the one-two-eight disaster last year, the city's merchants were devastated and have not yet been approved for implementation of collection. The French Concession is also within the Shanghai area, and now there is a so-called classified business donation, forcing the timber industry to pay it, which is actually destroying the integrity of the city's tax administration. It is reasonable to submit a report and request your government to review it, and give negotiations to prevent it, in order to maintain tax revenue and relieve merchants' difficulties, which is convenient for the public."

After the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Resolved the Layoff Issue 175

The Union Held a General Membership Meeting Yesterday

Requesting Priority Hiring in the Future

Regarding the case of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Fifth Wharf laying off 101 employees, after the mediation of Executive Director Du Yuesheng and Director Yang Zhixiong, and the subsequent private issuance of severance pay of one month's salary per person by the two directors, the Fifth Wharf Union held a general meeting of laid-off members at 2:00 PM yesterday, chaired by Shan Xishou, who reported on the mediation process of the two directors Du and Yang. The meeting resolved: (1) To accept the mediation method and decide that the union will go to the board of directors to collect the severance pay on Monday; (2) When the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company hires new workers in the future, priority should be given to hiring the laid-off workers; (3) Nine people were selected to go to the board of directors on the 6th to make demands.

The home of Zhang Jinfa at No. 78 Zhexing Lane on Diswei Road, Zhabei, was having dinner at around 6:00 PM the night before last when three robbers suddenly pushed open the door and entered. Fire at a Neighboring Property of the Little World 184

Yesterday at 12:20 PM, the reed mat awning erected by Lu Xiangzhi at No. 252 Fuyou Road, inside the city, next to the Little World, was suddenly ignited by stray fireworks. In an instant, flames soared into the sky. Police officer Sun Fengshan of the First District, Second Precinct, reported to the fire department, which immediately dispatched a fire engine to the scene. They exerted their utmost efforts to extinguish the fire, which was finally put out at 12:30 PM. Fortunately, it was only the reed mats that quickly burned through, preventing a major disaster. The neighboring property suffered only minor damage. Afterwards, Officer Sun brought Lu Xiangzhi, the owner of the garden, to the First District, Second Precinct, for questioning. After questioning by Director Xu, Lu Xiangzhi confessed that the fire was started by fireworks. However, whether his statement is true remains to be verified, and the case should be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Seeking a Runaway Maidservant 185

Tao Meixiang, a woman from Jiangyin, also known as Jiu Mei, is 15 years old. She has been working as a maidservant at the Ji residence, No. 81 Anle Fang, Penglai Road, in the city. On the afternoon of October 30th, the girl suddenly disappeared. It is suspected that she was lured away by someone and abducted. The girl is petite, with a long, round face, a slightly dark complexion, and her hair has been cut short. She can speak Shanghai and Jiangyin dialects. When she left, she was wearing three layers of cotton-padded jackets, one pair of cotton-padded pants, and a black-grey checkered flannel jacket, dark green "Freedom Cloth" pants, black velvet embroidered cotton shoes, and a blue-grey wool scarf. The Ji residence is searching for her, but in vain. It is said that the Ji residence has always treated this girl very kindly and has stated that if she can be found, she will be sent back to her parents' home. They deeply fear that she has been lured away by bandits, leading to her downfall or wandering aimlessly, which would be regrettable.

Important Announcement

The Municipal Government Announces the Full Text of the Revised Factory Law 188

The full text of the Factory Law has recently been revised and passed by the Central Government and has been forwarded by the Ministry of Industry to the provincial and municipal governments for promulgation. The Municipal Government has approved the forwarding and officially promulgated it the other day. The full text is reproduced below:

Revised Factory Law

Chapter I: General Provisions Article 1: This law applies to factories that use powered machinery and regularly employ 20 or more workers. Article 2: The competent authority in charge of this law is the municipal government in cities and the county government in counties, unless otherwise specified. Article 3: Factories shall maintain a worker roster, registering the following information about the workers and submitting it to the competent authority for record: (1) Name, gender, age, native place, address; (2) Date of entry into the factory; (3) Type of work, hours, and remuneration; (4) Worker's physical condition; (5) Rewards and punishments received in the factory; (6) Type and cause of injury or illness. Article 4: Factories shall submit the following information to the competent authority once every six months: (1) Any changes to the worker roster in the preceding article; (2) Worker injuries and illnesses and their treatment; (3) Disaster-related matters and relief efforts; (4) Retired workers and the reasons for their retirement.

Chapter II: Child Labor and Female Labor Article 5: Factories shall not employ any male or female workers under the age of 14. Male and female workers aged 12 or above but under 14 who were already working in factories before the promulgation of this law may be granted a grace period by the competent authority when this law is implemented. Article 6: Male and female workers aged 14 or above but under 16 are considered child labor. Child labor shall only be engaged in light work. Article 7: Child labor and female labor shall not be engaged in the following types of work: (1) Handling explosive, flammable, or toxic substances; (2) Working in places where dust, powder, or toxic gases are dispersed; (3) Cleaning, oiling, inspecting, repairing, and attaching or detaching belts and ropes on dangerous parts of operating machinery or power transmission equipment; (4) Connecting high-voltage wires; (5) Processing molten minerals or slag; (6) Firing boilers; (7) Other work that is harmful to morals or dangerous.

Chapter III: Working Hours Article 8: The actual working hours for adult workers shall be eight hours per day in principle. If it is necessary to extend working hours due to local conditions or the nature of the work, the working hours may be extended to ten hours. Article 9: Factories adopting a day and night shift system shall change all worker shifts at least once a week. Article 10: In addition to the provisions of Article 8, working hours may still be extended due to natural disasters, incidents, or seasonal factors after obtaining the consent of the labor union. However, the total working hours shall not exceed twelve hours, and the total extended hours shall not exceed forty-six hours per month. Article 11: The working hours for child labor shall not exceed eight hours per day. Article 12: Child labor shall not work between 8:00 PM and 6:00 AM the following morning. Article 13: Female labor shall not work between 10:00 PM and 6:00 AM the following morning.

Chapter IV: Rest and Holidays Article 14: Workers who work continuously for five hours shall have at least half an hour of rest. Article 15: Workers shall have one day of rest in every seven days as a regular holiday. Article 16: All commemorative days that the National Government's laws and regulations stipulate should be holidays shall be granted as holidays. Article 17: Workers who continue to work in the factory for a certain period shall have special holidays, and the duration of the holidays is as follows: (1) Seven days per year for those who have worked in the factory for one year but less than three years; (2) Ten days per year for those who have worked in the factory for three years but less than five years; (3) Fourteen days per year for those who have worked in the factory for five years but less than ten years; (4) For those who have worked in the factory for more than ten years, one day shall be added to their special holidays each year, and the total number shall not exceed twenty days. Article 18: Wages shall be paid as usual during the rest days and holidays stipulated in Articles 15 to 17. If workers do not wish to take special holidays, they shall be paid additional wages for the holidays. Article 19: When the competent authority deems it necessary for military or public works, it may suspend workers' holidays.

Chapter V: Wages Article 20: The minimum wage rate for workers shall be based on the living conditions of workers in the factory's location. Article 21: Factories shall pay workers wages in the local full-value currency. Article 22: When working hours are extended in accordance with the provisions of Articles 10 and 19, wages shall be increased by 1.1 to 1.2 times the usual hourly wage. Article 24: Men and women who do equal work with the same effectiveness shall be paid equal wages. Article 25: Factories shall not deduct wages in advance from workers as a penalty for breach of contract or compensation. (To be continued)

Reader Advisory

Is My View on Suicide Correct? 189

| Letter from Mr. Ren Wangyue |

Many readers of this column who are contemplating suicide come to ask you, sir, for answers. And your answers are always these few words: "Suicide is not a thought that those of us with upward aspirations should have. It is the psychology of a cowardly and shameful person." True, of course, your answer is correct! But it cannot be generalized. For suicides that are truly out of necessity, we do not seem to be able to absolutely oppose them. At the very least, they have some considerable value.

There are several kinds of suicides that I do not oppose at all and even approve of: (1) There are people who commit suicide because their bodies are unhealthy and too weak, and they feel that they cannot do anything. They will spend their lives (until death) living a consumptive life of an invalid, without any production for the country. It is better to die. Sir, can you consider this kind of suicide, due to physical reasons, to be shameful? (2) There are also people who commit suicide because they are used by rich people and wealthy young masters, and they live a life of slavery, not eating enough, not dressing warmly, and working tirelessly all day long without rest. Living is more painful than dying. Is it just to come into the world to be used by rich people and wealthy young masters? To resist and break through the dark life of slavery is impossible. They do not have the freedom to live, but everyone has the freedom to die. Although this kind of suicide is the act of a weakling, it is also something done by people with thorough thinking. Sir, what do you think? (3) There are also people who are neurasthenic and feel that everything is painful and depressing. They feel that the world is empty, lonely, and isolated, with few sympathizers, almost none. Looking around, there are only cold shoulders, not a single confidant, not a single understanding and comforting person. They feel that there is no joy in life and are unwilling to live such a lonely and boring life, so they commit suicide without any hesitation, cutting themselves off from the world. Sir, do you think this expression of thorough pessimism has any considerable value?

As for suicides for losing love for a woman, for appearance... of course, I also think that these kinds of suicides have no value at all.

Finally, what I want to ask you to answer is that I am about to carry out the third type of suicide. Because my environment is poor, and I have some lofty ambitions, but I don't know how to socialize or flatter people. Sir, what should I do? I hope you can give me a detailed and complete reply. I would be very grateful!

Answer: In our view, all three types of suicide that you approve of should be opposed: Why? As long as a person has a sound mind and thought, even if he is blind, deaf, or lame, he has his own work efficiency, and he has the opportunity to do his best for society. If he wants to commit suicide "because his body is unhealthy and too weak," frankly speaking, most Chinese people would have to commit suicide. Because there are very many Chinese people who are unhealthy. If compared with the physique of Westerners, eight or nine out of ten are "too weak." If we were in this situation, we should pursue the social causes and physiological and hygienic reasons for "unhealthy bodies" and "too much weakness," and fight against them. Even if we sacrifice ourselves for this, we would still leave behind our deeds and experiences for future generations. Compared to his passive suicide, it is truly immeasurable. This is the reason why we oppose the first type of suicide you mentioned. As for slaves of masters, if they cannot bear the suffering and oppression, from the master's point of view, it is best for you to commit suicide, so as not to trouble him. "Freedom" is truly freedom! However, this kind of freedom is only the most "thorough" act of unconditional submission by the slave to the master. If one uses this kind of freedom to defend his own attitude of unconditional submission, then it is a shameless mentality. As for you saying "to resist and break through the dark life of slavery, but it is impossible," why is it impossible? How has he ever "resisted"? How did he plan to "break through" their "dark life of slavery"? Please tell me! You must know that the dark life of slavery is formed by the dark forces of an oppressive society and an unequal society. To break this dark force, one must combine the extremely great and extremely resolute revolutionary forces in society, and accumulate extremely long and extremely valuable struggle experiences, and have an extremely strong and extremely stable war organization to achieve success. Now there is a group of people, perhaps self-proclaimed very intelligent people, who can rattle off many words like equality, freedom, civilization, barbarism, breaking, overthrowing, struggle, etc., as if they are revolutionary heroes and good fighters. However, once they come into contact with the dark forces, they abandon their armor and weapons and flee, drooping their heads and losing their spirits, with no positive spirit at all. If the dark forces were really as easy to break as they imagined, then wouldn't they all have become heroes in history? Let me tell you a story: "In the eighth year of King Wei, Chu sent a large army to attack Qi. The King of Qi sent Chunyu Kun to Zhao to ask for reinforcements, with a hundred gold coins and forty carriages and horses. Chunyu Kun looked up to the sky and laughed loudly, and the strings of his crown broke. The King said, "Is it too little, sir?" Kun said, "How dare I." The King said, "Is there a reason for laughing?" Kun said, "Now I came from the east and saw a man ploughing the field by the road, holding a pig's trotter and a cup of wine, and praying: 'Let the 甌 be full of 篝, let the 汚邪 be full of carts, let the five grains be abundant and ripe, let the 穰穰 be full of the house.' I saw that what he held was small but what he desired was extravagant, so I laughed at him." (Records of the Grand Historian, Biographies of the Knights-Errant) If you want to break through the shackles of slavery, you have to risk your life, and you have to fight this force decisively without yielding, one after another. The master will always have a day to collapse. If you fantasize about the liberation of the slave's status all day long, but dare not engage in a life-and-death struggle with the master, then it is "holding little but desiring much." Day and night, bowing and praying, begging for God's mercy and the master's favor to give you liberation is certainly a foolish and pitiful thought. Even if you commit suicide out of boredom, in the master's eyes, it is just the death of a dog. Good, a useless dog died! Can this be considered freedom? The slave's freedom is won, not given by others: the slave's freedom is the freedom to live, not the freedom to commit suicide. The slave who commits suicide not only cannot escape the dark life in the human world, but even if there is a heaven and hell, he will still be beaten in hell. Because the society of humans and ghosts is the same. If you cannot fight in the human world, then you are still a coward in the underworld, and you will still be a slave to the strong! Haha! If slaves want to commit suicide, we still have to advise them to wait and see! If you think about it calmly, is this kind of suicide "done by people with thorough thinking"? What does "thorough" actually mean? This is the reason why we oppose the second type of suicide you mentioned. "Feeling that everything is painful and depressing," why? "Feeling that the world is empty... there are almost no sympathizers," why? What do you think is not painful? High carriages and fat horses? Abundant food and clothing? Proud wife and beautiful concubines? What do you think is not empty? Becoming an official and reaching the chairman's position? Getting rich and becoming as wealthy as Hardoon? What kind of amazing person do you think you are, and why should anyone sympathize with you? What knowledge and talent do you have that can arouse people's sympathy? Is your speech genius? Is your literature a great creation? Do you have any inventions? Do you have any outstanding and amazing skills? Please ask yourself, and I guarantee you will sweat like rain and return in vain. Sure enough, in the end, the truth came out: you want to commit suicide because you "have a poor environment and some lofty ambitions, but you don't know how to socialize or flatter people." Isn't this the truth? It can be seen that you just can't stand "poverty," and in your view, the reason for this "poverty" is because you "don't know how to socialize or flatter people." This is really a pity in your eyes. Why do you say "don't know how"? If you knew how, wouldn't all the problems be solved? Poverty would be gone, emptiness would be gone, depression would be gone, and naturally you would change from a suicide addict to a lover of life! However, from the social point of view, your not knowing how to flatter people is precisely the happiness of society, because there is one less black sheep in the crowd. If you have this intention, then your suicide would be of no consequence to society. This reply of mine, which is sometimes happy, sometimes angry, and sometimes scolding, may seem inhuman, but in reality, I immediately saw the psychology of a petty-bourgeois intellectual full of the desire to succeed by chance and yet passively disappointed. If I don't break it thoroughly for you, it would be very dangerous. Please think calmly, can any of the three types of suicidal psychology you mentioned escape our previous answer: "Suicide is not a thought that those of us with upward aspirations should have. It is the psychology of a cowardly and shameful person"? If our answer does not satisfy you, please teach us again so that we can discuss it.

Luoyang Military Branch School to Enroll Students During Summer Vacation 193

Organizational Outline Approved

Education Bureau Approves Half Exemption of Advertising Tax for Establishment and Enrollment of Schools 195

Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Submitted to the Municipal Government

Municipal Education Association Notifies All Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Association, in order to facilitate the establishment of schools approved in the city, has requested the Public Utilities Bureau to exempt the advertising tax and handling fees. Yesterday, it received a reply from the Public Utilities Bureau, approving the exemption of half of the advertising tax. A special notice is hereby given to all schools. Yours sincerely, The second meeting of the Council of this Association resolved to send a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Public Utilities Bureau requesting the exemption of advertising tax and handling fees for the establishment of schools "approved for establishment" by this city's Education Bureau. It was approved in the reply letter: "Received your letter of December 12, 21st year, requesting the exemption of advertising tax and handling fees for the establishment of schools "approved for establishment" by the Education Bureau. After consultation with the Education Bureau, it is believed that the "approved for establishment" schools, although they are a necessary stage in the process of registration, the quality of their content and whether all proceedings comply with laws and regulations must be gradually examined and evaluated. It is different from the situation of "registered", "trial run" and "improved" schools that are stipulated for tax exemption. It is planned to exempt half of the advertising tax. Schools that have been approved for establishment but delay the registration procedures shall be taxed in accordance with the regulations to show restrictions. Also, the handling fee item should still be charged in accordance with the regulations. The Municipal Government's Order No. 4732 was consulted and approved. This is specially replied to for your information, etc.". This is hereby notified, and I hope you will check it.

Western League Class A Ever-Victorious Team 4-0 Eastern China Wins Cleanly Against Westerners' Club 203

The result became one-sided

The situation was very tense

The Eastern China football team, known as the ever-victorious team in the Western League Class A competition, yesterday won 4-0 cleanly against the Westerners' Club at the baseball field. This victory adds another page to their record book for this season.

Eastern China Team

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Guan Xun'an, Tu Kaiyuan, Feng Yunyou, Wu Youliang, Wan Xianghua, Chen Hongguang, Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Yutian

Shanghai Club

Ke Jin, Mole, Stoke, Xuefu, Boqisi, Hentesheng, Ke'erqiao, Jinmubo, Kenaer, Haitelai, Weifu

The Royal Army's Remaining Power Still Exists 204

The results of the two teams differed greatly, but the battle situation was tense. Although the Westerners' Club lost, their performance was excellent. Within ninety minutes, they gave Eastern China a deep blow. The team was purely English, and consisted of veteran players. In their glory days, they called themselves the Royal Army. Their left wing, Ke'erqiao, was one of the famous generals in the past. Others, such as Stoke and Xuefu, are also top-notch talents, and Mr. Shi's prestige still exists today. However, due to old age and lack of training, they often feel weak in the final stage of the game, which is regrettable.

The Ever-Victorious Team Preserves Its Honor 205

Eastern China cleanly scored four goals, preserving the honor of being ever-victorious. The four goals came about in different ways. Central defender Feng Yunyou opened his goal-scoring record for this season and scored the first goal, which was a pleasant surprise. Wan Xianghua followed up, thanks to Li Yichen's pass. Chen Jiaqiu struck with a lightning-fast shot, making the third goal. Chen Yutian went solo and broke into the goal, completing the four goals. However, Eastern China remained unscathed despite the fierce attack from the opposing team, which must be attributed to the dedication of the internal personnel. In the last forty-five minutes of the second half, the Shanghai Club's power was at its peak, just like Eastern China's in the first half, but the ending was different, which was due to Eastern China's internal guards being more outstanding.

Central Defender Feng Establishes a Remarkable Achievement First 206

When the two armies met, Eastern China's initial attack was unfavorable and they were forced to retreat. Veteran Ke'erqiao used his wit and cleverly crossed the ball. Kenaer and Haitelai were two ambushers waiting for the opportunity to launch an attack. Unexpectedly, Li Ning jumped up and headed the ball out, resolving the danger. Then, he led the army to counterattack. Li Yichen flicked the ball to the right, and Chen Yutian met it with his foot. Chen Jiaqiu did not want the credit and stepped aside. The enemy's eyes were immediately confused. Feng Yunyou had keen eyes and made a decisive decision, sweeping the ball out on the ground, heading towards the lower corner. Ke Jin was unable to stoop down and the ball went straight into the net. More than three thousand spectators applauded and cheered in unison, congratulating Feng's success.

Generals Xiang and Chen Achieve Success Again 207

With the opening of Eastern China's record, the military's morale became stronger. The five generals successively broke into the battle. In less than ten minutes, Feng Yunyou directed the entire army and came from all directions. Li Yichen took the lead, and Chen Jiaqiu responded effectively. The enemies dodged and defended. A ball flew to the left, landing in an empty spot. Wan Xianghua greeted the ball and shot, breaking through the enemy's gate again. Western veteran Ke'erqiao, witnessing his team's successive defeats, was ambitious and sent the ball out. Central defender Boqisi responded in the middle and sent a long ball, with a height difference of about a foot. Wan Xianghua was active on the left flank. Stoke personally came to the rescue. Wan used a feint to lure the tiger away from the mountain, giving a secret signal and passing the ball to the middle. Chen Jiaqiu got up and met the ball, avoided Mole, and went straight for the enemy's goal, completing a miraculous feat. With three goals in hand, the Westerners were successively defeated, and their spirits did not weaken. Ke'erqiao was still tireless, and the three generals in the middle also rushed forward. At that time, Zhou, the goalkeeper, greeted the ball high and low, doing whatever he wanted, and overcoming all kinds of difficulties. In the end, he took the lead with three to zero in the first half.

The Entire Team Mobilizes to Maintain the Winning Situation 208

Changing formations and fighting again, the Westerners were eager for revenge. The three armies advanced together, surrounding from all sides. Eastern China dispatched troops and generals to guard the key points. Li Ning and Guan Xun'an assisted Zhou in defending the goal, while Wu Youliang, Feng Yunyou and Tu Kaiyuan obstructed from all sides. Sometimes the two inside forwards also joined the defensive ranks, while the two wings and the center forward formed a triangle, stationed outside the border to prepare for a counterattack. Sure enough, in less than five minutes, Chen Yutian secretly crossed the river, penetrating deep into the hinterland and scoring a goal on the ground, gaining comfort in a dangerous situation. Eastern China's joy can be imagined. However, the situation was still tense, and the Westerners still had the upper hand, clearly holding a strong aura. When Li Yichen left the game due to injury, the dull situation turned clearer. Eastern China fought against the enemy with a team of ten people, resulting in a balanced situation. Wan Xianghua, Chen Jiaqiu and Chen Hongguang pounced on the enemy's goal repeatedly. Although they did not score, the enemy's momentum gradually faded. In the end, Eastern China regained the glory of the golden age, and their actions were free and unfettered in front of the Westerners' goal. As the battle ended, Eastern China won cleanly by four to zero.

Chinese Swimming Research Association Opens Heated Swimming Pool 215

Will Place Mirrors... Can See Posture

During each summer, there are thousands of people who float and play in the water every day. Such water enthusiasts, in addition to being active for a quarter of the year, can only sigh at the pool when autumn and winter arrive. Beginners often give up halfway, and even those who are proficient in this skill lack continuous practice, making it difficult to improve their results. Swimming enthusiast Yu Binqi and others have spared no effort in promoting swimming. Since they received the support of the Social Affairs Bureau of the Municipal Party Department in the 18th year of the Republic of China (1929) to establish the Chinese Swimming Research Association, it has been four years. Every summer, the association is responsible for free guidance, and as a result, hundreds of people have learned to swim, aiming to arouse the interest of people in society and to seek to popularize this skill. They have also worked hard to remedy the shortcomings of only being limited to the summer, which can be said to be aspiring to succeed. It is heard that they have agreed with Huang Sen, the curator of the Huang Ke Gymnasium, to jointly build a heated swimming pool in the gymnasium to benefit water enthusiasts. Wang Jianxin, a swimming enthusiast, invented mirrors installed in the pool, so that learners can correct their posture and voluntarily perform their movements to increase interest. The pool is currently under construction, and from now on, swimming enthusiasts can be said to have found their place. The association has also invited famous swimmers from Shanghai to join the guidance, guaranteeing that members will learn various styles. The association's address is on the third floor of No. 9 Sanma Road, inside the China Industrial and Commercial Company.

Chronicle

Shanghai Idle Talk 218

— Zhongxian

Noble and Mean

Wealth and nobility are originally two linked things. When a person becomes noble, their family property will naturally become wealthy. Those who become rich suddenly will gradually become noble. In ancient times, titles and salaries were considered noble, but modern people do not care about this. Those with money are the noble people, the so-called "tycoons" are the noble people of Shanghai.

Modern Chinese noble people mostly own real estate in Shanghai, so they can be considered Shanghai citizens. These are the fixed noble people. Shanghai is the transportation hub between the north and the south, east and west, and is a must-pass place for Chinese and foreign noble people. The upper, middle and lower class hotels are filled with thousands of past, future and current aristocratic travelers. These are the mobile noble people. The fixed noble people are the warp, and the mobile noble people are the weft, weaving together to form Shanghai's aristocratic society. When we open our eyes and take a look, we see that everyone coming and going is a noble person.

While there are many noble people in Shanghai, there are also quite a few mean people. The streetwalkers soliciting customers only cost three or four silver dollars a night, and the price can be said to be extremely low. These are still the obvious mean people. Hidden in the dark corners of society, there are still various unexpected mean people, such as "human and animal spectacles," "male prostitutes," and secret shows for people to watch, etc., all of which are special products of the aristocratic society.

The lives of Shanghai people can be worth more than 100,000 yuan (based on life insurance). Poor people who are run over by cars are sometimes only worth twenty or thirty yuan. The difference in the value of Shanghai people is also very considerable!

Overthrow Lethargy 219

— Yongzi

｜Make Day into Night｜

Lethargy must be avoided at all costs. When a person becomes deeply lethargic, no matter what they do, they are "lukewarm," and all their energy is nothing more than "getting by." Because people with deep lethargy are not far from death, and they do not know if they will still be alive tomorrow, they are happy to "drink today and get drunk today." Nineteen out of ten ministers and prime ministers in the late Qing Dynasty were from the imperial examination system. By the time they climbed up step by step from being a successful candidate in the imperial examinations to being a member of the Imperial Academy, they were, frankly speaking, qualified to enter the ancestral hall. Asking these old antiques who are approaching the end of their lives to transform China is simply like asking an old lady who cannot leave her room to design 20th-century new clothes. Therefore, in the current National Government, apart from a few founding members of the party-state, there are very few office workers with gray hair and white beards. This is enough to show that to have a politically energetic administration, one should never ask lethargic people to do it.

"The plan for the year lies in the spring, and the plan for the day lies in the morning." These two sentences fully show that we cannot lightly let go of the word "morning." Our normal office hours are from 9 am to 5 pm. In fact, 9 am is already close to noon and there is no such thing as "morning." By the afternoon, the sun is setting in the west, and it is full of "lethargy." Working during these office hours will certainly not produce anything full of "energy." So now I have a suggestion that is ignorant of propriety, which I would like everyone to consider: change the office hours to be from 2 am to 10 am. During these eight hours, it gradually turns from darkness to light, and the importance of "energy" cannot be overstated.

"Lethargy" covers the earth, and everyone is asleep in their dreams. When there is "energy," everyone gets up to work. I think this method may be able to eliminate all the lethargy in society today and generate a thriving atmosphere. If we always muddle through and sleep during the energetic hours and work in lethargy, then don't even think about changing "the old China" into "the young China!"

Confucius Goes Abroad 220

— Lai Chengyuan

｜Zilu is Confused｜

In the Spring and Autumn Period, Confucius became angry because his philosophy was not being practiced, and in a fit of anger, he wanted to go abroad to live for a few years. If he found an opportunity, he would make a comeback! But although he shouted loudly, his feet were still not moving. In fact, his old man was just venting his anger and putting on a stern face, deliberately moving people's feelings. He also knew how dangerous it was to go abroad! The wind and waves are very big, and the voyage is turbulent. At such an old age, recklessly fighting with the God of the Sea is sure to be like hitting a rock with an egg! It's laughable that Zilu was so foolish that he believed it to be true, as if he would follow the Master abroad, and without him, it would not work! Confucius saw that he was so pitifully confused and did not understand the innate mysteries in his (Confucius') belly, and he sighed and said, "You, you are braver than I am, but you have nothing to draw on!"

From this alone, we can prove that the people of ancient times, apart from the fact that Old Kong was able to act young and smart, most of the rest were extremely simple-minded. Isn't the issue of going abroad a good example? If Zilu were born thousands of years later, and the Master was making a fuss about going abroad, he would have a flash of inspiration and come up with a plan. He could use radio broadcasting to say, "If the Master wants to go abroad, I, You, will not allow it. When the barbarians invade, we will keep him to be used by the country!" Anyway, the Japanese soldiers have not yet attacked Shandong (Lu), and firing a few cannon shells without medicine for the people to eat a few empty glutinous rice balls might win him the title of hero, right?

Lin Gengbai's Poem 221

Hearing Rain at Midnight

The remnants of the night are long and like raindrops, a singing voice breaks the dream and comes from the corner of the house. The sickbed is quiet, the upper floor is entering meditation, and the sound of racing cars and wind call out in the night. It is difficult to share the thousand sorrows with those who have passed away, are there any in the world who can pity this intention? I remember Salome in my life, the moonlight dripping blood to bury her head.

Feelings Written in Sickness

The smell of medicine and the sound of bells depend on each other, can we share the door with you when the rain comes? (Yi Ping is uniquely clear, but in vain) Former friends who were easily angered become more noble in office, and lovers who were relegated to leisure are rare to hear from. The sound of the piano and singing in the courtyard urge sorrow, and the shadow of the flowers should give some comfort. I chat and boast by the plum blossoms, and I have only known a few things in my life.

Further Discussion on Ornaments 222

— Guo Lanxin

| What Benefit to the Nation?

In government offices, female employees have the nickname "red flower vase," meaning they lack ability and are merely decorative. However, not all female employees can be tarred with the same brush; some are quite capable. Speaking of ornaments, many women in our cities willingly become ornaments, catering to the pleasures of those who admire them. They are draped in Western silks and satins, masking their natural beauty with excessive powder, perfume, eyebrow pencil, and lipstick for artificial embellishment. Simultaneously, they largely gravitate towards materialistic pleasures. Some willingly sell their bodies, bowing to money and exchanging their flesh for enjoyment. They crave grand Western-style houses, automobiles, pianos, high-heeled shoes, silk stockings, fashionable clothing, luxurious accessories, velvet carpets, delicacies, American flags, Golden Delicious apples, chocolates, wine, and curaçao, frequenting cinemas, dance halls, parks, hotels, and clubs. I ask you, what benefit are such citizens, male or female, to the nation?

Ultimately, should one strive to be a useful person or willingly become a lifeless ornament? If you were to ask anyone, they would all say they want to be useful, but superfluous ornaments abound before our eyes, and some still tread down this path of degradation and ruin. I cannot help but feel boundless sorrow!

Fiction

Photograph 224

— Mo Yi

"Xiaorong, eat faster! Your bowl of rice is getting cold," Zhang Rongjiu's wife scolded her five-year-old son, urging him to eat his rice and not just the vegetables.

"The snow is so heavy again. How will we get to Brother Tong's place in Qianjinbao later? Someone brought a message yesterday saying he needed to discuss something important with me and that I should definitely go today, but... Who is it?... A knock on the door... Could it be Brother Tong himself?... "

Zhang Rongjiu listened attentively to the knocking sound.

"Brother Tong is too impatient! With such heavy snow and a strong wind, he still comes over... It must be urgent. Listen... the knocking is so hurried..." Zhang Rongjiu's brother said, getting up to open the door.

"Ouch... What are you doing?... Why are you hitting people?... Who is it?... Bastards... That hurts..."

Zhang Rongjiu's brother had barely opened the door when he was struck with a rifle butt. Because the snow and wind were blowing in, he couldn't open his eyes and retreated to the side, cursing as he looked at the people who had hit him. He saw two enemies in yellow uniforms and a Chinese man in plain clothes.

"Damn it, why didn't you open the door faster? If we hit you, what can you do to us? Hurt? Hmph, serves you right!... If you curse again, we'll beat you to death!" The Chinese man in plain clothes pointed at him and shouted.

"..." He didn't dare to reply.

"Go inside! What are you standing here for?"

He didn't even close the door but led them inside. Zhang Rongjiu was already standing at the door, looking outside.

"The Japanese army is going to use this village for combat exercises. You should quickly hide in the ravines of Pingdingshan Mountain. Don't stay here and get shot! Later, Emperor Xuantong will even give you money to reward you handsomely for the use of your land..." the Chinese man said.

"Please wait a moment. Let us finish our meal before we go," Zhang Rongjiu pleaded with a smile.

"Go... Go... No... No..." The two enemies scowled, mimed hitting people with their guns, and mumbled irregular Chinese words. (4)

Children's Paradise

Pigeons Take Pictures 225

— Yun

Modern science is so advanced. The equipment used on the battlefield is truly amazing. For example, dogs are used to scout for the enemy, pigeons are used to deliver letters, and, most remarkably, Germany used pigeons to take photographs during the Great War. The pigeon photography method involved attaching an automatic camera to the pigeon's chest. When the pigeon flew over enemy lines, the camera was activated by the movement of the pigeon's claws, automatically capturing the enemy's position. Therefore, when aircraft were unavailable for reconnaissance, pigeons could be used instead. However, training military pigeons is very difficult.

Animal Child-Rearing Methods 227

— Chu

(1) Kangaroos: Kangaroos, native to Australia and the South Pacific islands, carry their young in a pouch after birth. The pouch contains four nipples, providing the young with food and warmth while protecting them from various external dangers. This is the most peculiar method of child-rearing among mammals.

(2) Surinam Toads: A type of South American toad, the Surinam toad, has brood pouches on the female's back resembling honeycombs. After the female lays her eggs, the male transfers them to the pouches. When the tadpoles are fully developed, they hop out of the pouches one by one.

(3) Sticklebacks: When sticklebacks are about to spawn, the male gathers aquatic plant stems and builds a circular nest in preparation for the female to lay her eggs. This fish lives in cold-water rivers. After the female lays her eggs, the male guards the nest. While the female is away foraging, the male spreads his pectoral fins to protect the eggs and sometimes wags his pectoral fins to flush out dirty water and introduce fresh water into the nest, making this fish the most unique of its kind.

(4) Spider Sacs: The spider's hind legs have a sac that it clings to and refuses to separate from. If someone tries to take the sac, it would rather injure itself and desperately protect it because the sac is filled with eggs.

(5) Potter Wasps: Potter wasps build bottle-shaped nests made of mud on tree branches for raising their young. After the female lays her eggs, both the male and female wasps guard the nest.

The Difficulty of Working Capital Turnover in Shanghai 234

The Shanghai business community has always relied on the financial sector's lending for the transfer of working capital. This year, money shops are particularly cautious, and they carefully consider the opening of accounts. They refuse to renew accounts that have even the slightest dissatisfaction, and new accounts cannot be easily established unless they are solid and have excellent credit. Therefore, at the time of submitting accounts, each business considers obtaining a money shop account as a precious treasure. This shows the difficulty of working capital turnover in various industries this year.

(Factory Demand Remains Cautious) Current cotton demand remains sluggish. Sources include 500 bales of Yaohua cotton and Shaanxi cotton 31.50. Shenxin Factory imported 200 pieces. Warehoused Taicang cotton 31.50. Zhenxin Factory imported 400 bales to Wuxi.

Tongzhou and Chongming Cottonseed Trading Exceeds 1,000 Dan 238

Since the New Year, there has been very little cottonseed trading. Recently, some shipments from Tongzhou and Chongming arrived, totaling over 1,000 dan, which were traded yesterday. The price remained at $2.70, but due to the current situation, market sentiment is very weak, and prices may decline slightly. This price has been able to hold steady because there is not much inventory in the interior.

U.S., British, and Indian Cotton All Rebound 239

Yesterday, U.S. cotton rebounded due to positive news from Liverpool, which spurred buying. The market was strong and active, with futures rising by 10 to 12 points and spot prices rising by 10 points. British cotton futures rose by 7-8 points, and spot prices rose by 1 point. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 7 points. Indian cotton initially rose due to strong short covering, then weakened due to merchant selling, but ultimately strengthened again due to positive news from Liverpool. Fair American rose by 2 rupees, Oomra rose by 2.25 rupees, and White Western rose by 2.5 rupees. Original telegraph record left. (3rd Day Telegram)

U.S. New Cotton Acreage to Increase by 10% 240

| No Certainty in Rural Relief and War Debt Issues |

New York, 3rd Day Telegram, Report on the cotton market for the week: Last week, the cotton market closed on a bullish note, with some selling by short positions. Pressure from the South did not increase. Powerful players appeared to be accumulating, but prices stopped rising. Currently, there is no progress in Congress regarding the issuance of paper money, and there is no certainty about relief and war debt issues. Furthermore, the political situation in Germany is causing pessimism. Sales are occurring in the mainland and the Far East (including Bombay). However, China is buying spot goods in the South when prices fall. News from Washington: Congress recently passed a bill directing President Hoover to provide 350,000 bales of cotton from the Bureau of Agricultural Economics' inventory to the Red Cross and other charitable organizations for clothing the poor. Spring planting preparations have begun. Soil conditions are excellent, but many boll weevils have been found. Industry insiders predict that cotton acreage will increase by 3% to 10%. It is reported that the 619,000 bales of raw cotton stockpiled by the Bureau of Agricultural Economics, which were previously used as collateral for agricultural loans, have now been approved for this purpose.

The Origin of the Sluggishness of Grain and Rice Markets 242

Customers Haven't Arrived, Market Movement Must Wait Until After the Lantern Festival

Bargain-Priced Foreign Wheat Affecting Flour and Wheat Markets

(Shanghai South Rice Market Has Abundant Supply but Sluggish Sales) Yesterday's supply came from over 40 firms in Puzhong, with inventory accumulating due to several days of increased supply and slow sales. In addition, retail sales are stagnant. Although wholesale merchants have over 1,000 piculs of goods in warehouses, the market remains weak. Su Tong, Nangang, Qingjiao, and other types of rice continued to fall in price by 20 cents. Although Du Yangjian and Yinyuan are scarce, they are not as tight as the previous day. Therefore, prices have fallen slightly. Factories only released Yangjian, with prices remaining unchanged. Changbang rice from inland rivers could not arrive due to frozen conditions.

(Shanghai North Rice Market Has Stagnant Sales and Falling Prices) Yesterday, over 10 boats arrived from the lower reaches of the river. Both white japonica and thin japonica rice sales were sluggish, and the market was down by 22-30 cents. Although there was only a small arrival of thin japonica early rice, retail sales were sluggish and wholesale remained stagnant. Prices also fell by 30 cents. A small amount of Yang Du Jian arrived, and sales were acceptable, with prices down slightly. Port Jian was scarce, Ke Jian was weak, and Yinyuan had few arrivals and slow sales, with prices down by 22-30 cents. White Yuan was weak, with a drop of over 10 cents.

(Passenger Xian Rice Continues to Have Some Sales) The Passenger Xian rice market saw both arrivals and sales were slow. However, both local and outside buyers are willing to deal which is helping maintain the price. However, it will be difficult to see market activity for now, but we expect some activity from buyers after the Lantern Festival. Yesterday, 445 bags of Fuzhou refined Yuan rice were sold at $10.048 to $10.045 per bag. Local dealers also purchased 340 bags of Jiangxi late rice at $9.15 to $8.82. Local dealers exclusively handled 230 bags of Hunan red rice at $8.65 to $8.55.

(Foreign Merchants Hawking No. 1 Saigon Rice) Foreign rice stocks remained stagnant. There was slight interest in the market, but because cargo owners insisted on high prices, most buyers switched to Passenger Xian rice. However, after receiving this news, foreign merchants were actively promoting their products in the market. Yesterday, Yuanli received a telegraph from March/April offering No. 1 Saigon rice at 4.3 yuan. Traders are considering the offer, but there were no transactions that day.

(Soybean Sales Acceptable, Oilcake Sales Showing Activity) The miscellaneous grains market remained quiet. Huangdou Chefang and factories continued to purchase soybeans, with 4 train cars of soybeans traded. Local dealers purchased 2 train cars of Dalian soybeans. The Fuzhou group purchased over 400 bags of Chongming Shayang soybeans. High-quality soybeans are stable, while medium- and low-quality soybeans remain weak. Oilcake sales are showing activity, and prices may rise. Nanjing Gangdou is stable due to continued inquiries. Although there were inquiries about foreign sesame, there were no transactions, but sporadic sales continued and the market remained stable. Raw peanuts are killing higher grade products, and peanuts are firm.

(Flour Market Again Shows Uniform Decline) Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, all months showed a uniform decline. Foreign wheat prices fell by another 10 cents. Since the market opened, actual sales to customers have been exceptionally quiet. All activity was limited to small transactions. Prices in Tianjin were also falling, from $2.90 to $2.80 yesterday. Bargain-priced Australian wheat continued to flood the market. It is reported that foreign firms were offering forward contracts at $3.50, so the future volatility of the market will be unavoidable. As a result, market sentiment became very weak, and prices for all months softened. Small factories also began to withdraw from the market. Although total trading volume was only over 200,000, market sentiment was extremely pessimistic. It is predicted that prices may fall to $1.80 in the near future. As a result, February and March contracts fell by 1.75 cents compared to the previous day, April contracts fell by 1.25 cents, May contracts fell by 1 cent, June contracts fell by 1.5 cents, and July contracts fell by 1.25 cents.

(Wheat Futures Cleared, Little Improvement in Market) Yesterday, trading in wheat futures was extremely quiet in the morning, with only a few transactions in the May contracts. Trading was more active after the market opened in the afternoon, but prices trended lower. The continued offering of Australian wheat at $3.50 kept market sentiment weak. Near-term and distant-term contracts were unstable. Due to foreign wheat, sellers were eager to dispose of the July new wheat contracts. As for the current month, there is a risk that the situation will change if factories do not accept the foreign wheat used for hedging. As a result, this month's contracts fell by 2 cents from the previous day, March contracts fell by 3 cents, April contracts fell by 4 cents, and July contracts fell by 2 cents.

According to Friday's telegram from Chicago, wheat prices fell due to weakness in securities and selling from the East. Total trading volume for the two days was 10 million bushels. The closing prices for the 3rd are listed below:

Sugar Market - Raw and White Sugar Slightly Soft 243

Yesterday, the sugar market was flat overall, with spot prices slightly lower and the Dutch exchange rate rising. The Public Association's prices were 15 taels 6 qian 7.5 fen for No. 24 raw white sugar, down 2.5 fen, with limited trading. There was no change in No. 18 and No. 20 medium white sugar. No. 8, 9 and 10 Dutch red sugar were slightly firmer. On the foreign side, Changxing offered several hundred bags of No. 16 medium white sugar at 14 taels 7 qian, and Huaxin continued to offer raw red sugar at 14 taels 1 qian. In futures, Lijii and Yihe sold 200 tons and 100 tons of sugar respectively in February-March deliveries, all at 4.2 Dutch currency. Tianxiang also sold 200 tons of medium white sugar, February-March shipment prices at 3.85 Dutch currency. Diao Qing's Jian Group has sold a total of 1,100 bags in the past few days, with prices all at 9 taels 6 qian (full weight, clear skin). Chao Group's Chaoqing continued to sell at the original price with slight continuations, and the new cotton red market showed slight fatigue, but it was difficult to ease up.

The Agreement on Jian Ice Exchange Regulations Has Been Resolved 244

Only Awaiting Implementation Notice from Both Parties Today

The implementation of exchange regulations had been delayed for many days for Jian Ice due to the change of the city scale (weights). Yesterday, it was said that both parties had reached a compromise and we are printing the exchange regulations after the change of scale: (1) 82% of city scale equals 50 Shanghai Standard weight (2) No deductions for silver (3) Cargo is delivered against dealer slips (4) silver contracts are limited to 15 days, with silver due even if cargo is not delivered (5) Delivery limited to three months, with goods to be cleared (6) Fire insurance and warehouse rent are responsible by dealers.

Dried Goods Market: Daylily Inventory is Low, Price is Tight 245

Due to low inventory of dried lily flowers held by the trade, prices were tight as the trade held firm. Yesterday, the price rose by 1-2 taels with less than 100 bags being offered. Top-grade village daylilies were priced at 17 taels, country daylilies were priced at 15 taels 6 qian, and Xuzhou daylilies were priced at 15 taels. At the same time, market prices also followed higher. For example, the bidding for top-grade village daylilies was at 18 taels, followed by 16 taels to 15 and a half taels, and then 14 and a half taels. Old goods reached as high as 8 taels, and the next highest was 6 taels.

The Main Reason for the Soaring Price of Refined Antimony in the Hardware Market 246

Recently, the price of refined antimony has been exceptionally firm. The standard estimated price has reached 270 taels. It is said that the reasons for the price increase are partly due to the Communist bandits ravaging the production areas, resulting in extremely low arrivals, and partly due to the expansion of European sales in the local market, leading to a supply shortage, speculation by hoarding merchants, and monopoly by trading merchants, resulting in a sharp increase of more than 20 taels. It is said that over 20 tons were traded yesterday.

Copper and Tin Markets Remain Sluggish 247

The "copper" market has been sluggish recently, with extremely little trading. It has been found that the outlets for this commodity are copper coin bureaus and military factories, but these factories have not been making additional purchases recently. As a result, market sentiment is weak and prices are low. Currently, refined copper is estimated at 35 taels and yellow copper at 14 taels. "Tin ingots" were estimated at 95 taels 5 qian for Xiaohong yesterday, 104 taels for Fuzu, and 103 taels for Holland, with secondary grades all down by more than one tael. Aside from the Shaoxing group, there were no other buyers.

Business Sutra (5)

What Makes Good Walnuts? 248

Walnuts Have a Good Taste, and Are Inexpensive.

"Quality" Walnuts are also known as "Hetao." They are nutritious, sweet, and fragrant, and contain oil. Their outer skin is bitter. Their shells can be used as fuel. They are produced in Tianjin and other places. The standards for goods are generally: (1) large size; (2) white and thin shells; (3) abundant and white kernel; and (4) dry body. The quality of various goods is described below:

Hand-Picked Walnuts: Large and uniform in size, white and thin shells, abundant and dry kernel.

Dongchang Walnuts: Slightly varying in size, slightly thick white shells, abundant and dry kernel.

Changping Walnuts: Varying in size, slightly red and thick shells, abundant and dry kernel.

Pinggu Walnuts: Similar to Changping Walnuts.

Shimen Walnuts: Varying in size, thick shells with kernels embedded, less abundant kernel, dry body.

Haozhou Walnuts: Small in size, white and relatively thin shells, insufficient kernel, relatively soft body.

Dong Walnuts: Varying in size, slightly thick shells, insufficient white kernel, relatively soft body.

Shangluo Walnut Meat: White in color, mostly whole pieces, few fragments, dry body.

Tianjin Walnut Meat: Slightly the same.

Foreign Walnut Meat: Different ways of cracking. Whole kernels ("walnut balls") are the best, followed by halves, and then quarters. Must also be white in color and large in size to be qualified.

"Prevention of Spoilage" During the yellow plum season, those with soft bodies are prone to mold, oiliness, and insect infestation. Walnut meat, lacking the protection of the shell, is even more prone to spoilage. Therefore, during this period, some are stored in cold storage to avoid this issue, but this incurs high external costs. If the goods are low in cost and there is still hope, it can be more cost-effective. However, if there is prospect for high-priced goods, it can also protect the capital.

"Consumption Methods" Remove the shell and skin. (Easy to peel off after soaking in boiling water.) Fry with salt water to make "Salted Walnuts." Make with white sugar to make "Walnut Candy." Both taste delicious. For "Walnut Pastry," mix walnut meat and rock sugar in a small mortar and pound finely. Eat dry or mix with boiling water. Can also be eaten with good Shaoxing wine for a nourishing effect. Alternatively, stuff walnut meat into pitted longans or peeled and pitted black dates. These all have unique flavors. Other uses include pastries, dumplings, etc., all of which require them.

"Medicinal Use" The septum of the walnut (i.e., the layer in the walnut kernel) can be soaked in wine to treat back pain. (Errata) Yesterday's Business Sutra was (4), mistakenly printed as (3). We are correcting it.
