Free Talk

Strange Rickshaw Puller (2) (By G.K. Chesterton, Translated by Shi Heng) 272

I looked at the man. No ordinary dishonest rickshaw puller could come up with such a certain and unfounded lie. And this man was not a dishonest rickshaw puller. If ever there was a human face that was heavy, simple, humble, with two eyes sticking out like a toad's eyes, if ever there was (in short) a face that possessed all the essence of a human face, it was the face of this hateful and respectable rickshaw puller. I looked up and down the street; an unusual dim light seemed about to cover it. And in an instant, that old devil of skepticism poked his finger at my nerves again. What is certainty? Can anyone be certain of anything? Heavens! Thinking of the hackneyed tone of the skeptic who constantly asks us if we possess a past life. Whether we possess a past life is an exciting question for skepticism about truth. Purely theoretically speaking, what could it be other than a legend or a picture a minute ago? The darkness on the road became thicker. The rickshaw puller quietly recounted to me, from the strange moment I hailed him outside Euston Station, all my gestures, words, complex and consistent actions, how could I know (my skeptical friend would say) that I had not hailed him outside Euston? I was confirming my claim, and he was confirming his claim. He was clearly as honest a man as I was, and one who was doing a more respectable job. In that moment, the universe and the stars shook because of a hair's breadth of imbalance, and the foundations of the universe were moved. But for this very reason I believe in drinking, for this very reason I believe in free will, for this very reason I believe in the fixed nature of virtue, a reason that can only be explained by "saying I don't want to be a madman," I continued to believe that this honest rickshaw puller was wrong, and I repeatedly told him that I had indeed gotten in at the corner of Leicester Square. He began to say with the same certainty and deep innocence, "You were hailing me outside Euston Station, and you said ||"

But at this moment, his posture underwent an amazing transformation, as if he had lit a fire inside like a lamp. "Oh, please forgive me, sir," he said. "Please forgive me, please forgive me. You hired me from Leicester Square. I remember now. Please forgive me." With that, this strange man, with a sharp whistling sound, raised his whip and drove away, spinning the wheels. This whole scene, I dare swear by the flag of the British Empire, is absolutely true.

× × × ×

As he disappeared into the distance and the mist, I looked at this strange rickshaw puller. I imagined that although this man's face seemed very sincere, perhaps if viewed from behind he possessed an extremely evil devil-like temperament, which I do not know if it is correct. Perhaps he was sent to tempt me, who had defended the stubbornness of certainty in the daytime. But in any case, this event gave me a pleasant feeling of remembering my "sense of reality," although it had fallen for a moment, and stood up again. (The End)

Three Wishes for Saving the Country Through Aviation (By He Jiagan) 273

Now all sorts of people are shouting various ways to save the country, as if everyone suddenly loves their country. But that's not really the case. It was originally like this, they have been saving the country in this way, but now they are just shouting it out.

So the banker says saving the country through savings, the manuscript seller says saving the country through literature, the painter says saving the country through art, the dancer says saving the country by including it in entertainment, and, according to the tobacco company, smoking General Ma Zhanshan brand cigarettes is also a way to save the country.

These various ways of saving the country, like the previous ones that have already been implemented, will also be implemented in the future, and will definitely not last only five minutes.

Only saving the country through aviation is more unique and deserves a closer look. The future is also difficult to predict, because the people who advocate it are generally not aviators themselves.

Then, we might as well say a few words of hope in advance.

People who read Shanghai newspapers last year probably remember that didn't Suzhou have a team of planes that came to fight? Later, all the others "disappeared", leaving only the plane of the foreign martyr, who was overwhelmed by the Japanese planes and finally shot down, causing his mother to run all the way from America to weep bitterly, and take away a few wreaths. It is said that Guangzhou also had a team that set off, and young ladies embroidered poems on their shirts and gave them to the soldiers to encourage them on their journey. However, unfortunately, it seems that they have not arrived yet.

Therefore, we should state two hopes before the air defense team is established:

1. Recognize the road clearly,

2. Fly faster.

There is also a more important point, which is that we are now moving from "non-resistance" to "long-term resistance" and entering a time of "psychological resistance". In reality, we may not necessarily fight foreign countries for a while. At that time, the soldiers' skills are itching, but they have no place to show their heroism. I don't know if they will drop bombs on unarmed people? So we must still trembling state a hope, which is!

3. Don't kill the people!

Snowy Night 274

— Mei Kan

The cold snow fell, the time was already dusk, and the pedestrians and vehicles on the road could be said to be gone. A black cat in the apartment was dozing off at the foot of my bed. In such cold weather, in principle, a stove should be installed in the room, but this winter, I have not lit a stove. It's not that I am not afraid of the severe cold, but because my old Japanese fire pot met with disaster during the January 28th Shanghai Incident and had long been exposed as a corpse in a field of rubble near Fort Baoshan, Wusong. The tragic state of being smashed to pieces still makes me a little sad when I think about it now. Since then, I haven't bought another stove.

Suffering from rheumatism, I am prone to relapse when it gets cold. Fortunately, I have been doing well recently. Except for pain in my legs, the rest of my body is comfortable as usual. I can't help but thank God for his generosity!

Originally, on such a snowy day, it would be best to sit by the stove, enjoying peanuts with aged Shaoxing wine while whispering sweet nothings with a beautiful young woman. However, such a peaceful blessing is not for me. Although I love both wine and women, the so-called "marten fur coat for wine, golden house for a beauty" dream has not been realized in my whole life. Thinking about it, I can't help but feel a little melancholic!

I always have these wild thoughts, perhaps this is the inferiority of the petty bourgeoisie. My friends often scold me, and I often feel that I shouldn't think like this, but when I'm bored, I can't help but think about these things.

I am indeed too contradictory! Sometimes I curse myself like this. But I am determined not to hide my shortcomings from others. I believe that those who know me will naturally forgive me, and those who don't know me can scold me. To be a well-rounded person is actually quite troublesome. It is better to seek peace of mind, which is more convenient.

Night is approaching, and the entire room seems to be immersed in water. It is still snowing heavily outside. I predict that the snowy scenery tomorrow will be even more spectacular. The strong north wind is roaring outside the window, the glass window is trembling frequently, and the faint light waves of the electric lamp cannot reach every dark corner. The cold air is eroding my skin. I am sitting alone, surrounded by a desolate mood. After eating dinner, boredom still occupies my entire heart. After thinking about it, it is better to go to bed and sleep. The clock's hand is still dozing on the number eight, so I spread out the quilt and jump in to pretend to sleep.

Tossing and turning, tossing and turning, the quilt is still as cold as iron. I don't know where the warmth has dissipated to! I had long wanted to "sleep until dawn embracing the void," but who knew that I didn't even have this little bit of luck. It's so cold that I can't even sleep. I'm going to have insomnia again tonight!

Insomnia is extremely detrimental to rheumatism patients. Sure enough, my legs started to hurt again in the middle of the night.

The snores of the neighbors on the left and right are sounding proudly, but I still have no sleepiness. I stretch out my head to look at the black cat beside the bed, and it is already sleeping soundly. I can't help but feel a little jealous!

A Trip to Mount Luojia (3) 275

— Ms. Wen Juan

We also followed and stepped into the gate of the Guandi Temple, but it was full of desolation. Only a large well in the center of the courtyard still stood there majestically. Mr. C told us: "According to legend, this well is where Guan Gong of the Three Kingdoms led his army and struck the spring with his sword." Absurd myths are unfounded, but I stared at it in a daze. This clear well water once reflected my face five years ago, and it also reflected the face of another friend. | I bless his soul in heaven! At that time, it was mid-April, a rare holiday. We went out of the city for a walk and came to this place. Because we were thirsty, we drank tea in the tea house here and took a rest. Then we got up and walked around. In the small courtyard to the west, he climbed up a tree for me and broke off two beautiful hydrangea flowers. These complete flowers seemed to be admiring our active lives, opening their eyes and staring at me intently. We felt that being able to take the time to relive a little poetic life in such a tense day was a pleasure that was difficult to express. We promised each other: if we can retire to the countryside in the future, we will re-enact the story of riding a donkey on the lake. So we each recorded the day's travels in our diaries so that we could follow them again in the future. Who knew that leaving this remnant would only increase the material for today's sadness!

After turning around, I felt very bored, so I retreated and saw that the open stone road was still in the same condition as it was then, but all that was left by the roadside was not the lush green of early summer, but only the withered roots of flowers and plants. If the stone road had a memory, it should remember a scene from five years ago – a young man with a resolute expression and heroic spirit, and the image of a cheerful and healthy woman? However, the ruthless stone slab only gave me a cold answer. Its heart had been trampled numb by the violence of the world.

Only the affectionate grass was still shaking its haggard body in the west wind, as if greeting me. Ah, grass! You seem to know my thoughts, so you show your sad face to express sympathy with me? When we first met, you and I were both young, but now! You have been destroyed by the power of nature, and I have been deprived of the life in my life by the waves of the world. But, ah! When your youth is gone, there will be a time to come again; but for me, the dead cannot be resurrected, and the lost youth will never return.

Mr. C saw that I was silent and said, "You don't seem to like this place very much?"

"Yes, it's too desolate here."

The two young men looked surprised when they heard my words. They felt that I had always been the person who liked natural scenery the most, so why would I suddenly get tired of it! Who knew that my heart was already locked in sorrow at this time, and I could no longer say words of praise for nature!

But Mr. N shook off my reminiscence with his courageous spirit. He picked up a stone lion.

Only "strength"! Strong strength is the way out of everything, I understood. "Sadness is a sign of weakness. I don't want to settle for being in a weak position!" I thought in my heart, and unknowingly I had arrived at the bus station.

The lake and mountains sent us back on our way with a calm and meaningful smile, and the giant shadow of the long-distance bus broke through all the surrounding darkness. (End)

(Note 1) Built inside the East Gate of Wuchang when Zhang Zhidong was the governor of Hubei.

(Note 2) Hongshan is outside the East Gate, with a pagoda on it.

(Note 3) When Wuhan University was built, explosives were used to break through the mountain.

Long Creative Piece

Crossroads of the Times and Love (Continued) 276

— Zhang Ziping

The two of them turned back and walked west, and came to the famous M dance hall.

It was a little early, and the band hadn't taken the stage yet. Only five or six dancers who were probably not very popular had arrived. Two of them were practicing the blues while hugging each other, and the rest were just sitting blankly on their chairs.

The two of them also picked two seats and sat down. He felt that the dancing of the two dancers was quite artistic. He especially appreciated their foot stomping, which was very loud and had a rhythmic tone. So he told her.

"That's because your appreciation is too poor..."

She laughed again. What she meant was that the Chinese were generally neurasthenic and lacked the ability to appreciate. However, the Chinese art world, especially the literary world, puts the cart before the horse. Everyone starts with criticism first. As a result, they either fall into extreme subjective pickiness, or the critics themselves are arrogant, thinking that insulting other people's art can raise their own reputation. They really lack the effort of cultivation. This problem often reveals itself unconsciously in literature. Therefore, in order to achieve this cultivation, one must first start with the work of appreciation. She advised Haiquan to postpone taking a subjective attitude towards all art for the time being, and first take an objective appreciation attitude, and then there would be progress.

However, Haiquan still didn't quite understand, and was only surprised that this Japanese woman had such a deep study of art.

"Mr. Lin, are you good at dancing?"

"Not good."

He answered frankly. He had been to dance halls with his classmates several times before, but he just dragged his legs and was pulled around by the dancers. He was really afraid that Mrs. Tsuruko would see this ugly state. He decided to just appreciate it tonight.

The music started. Dancers and guests also came one after another. Every time the electric light dimmed, several more guests came. "Mr. Lin, let's have one too."

She pulled his hand, but he just smiled and didn't answer.

"See if she will stand up and pull me hard, that's how she shows her enthusiasm for herself... Ah, the opportunity to hug her has come!"

He was hoping like this. He thought that he would definitely not be a toad this time.

From holding hands to hugging the waist, from hugging the waist to hugging, from hugging to... to... ascending step by step, he thought that the love between the two of them would probably graduate soon.

Embracing the music, he dragged his long legs, which were like two hard bamboo tubes, and let Mrs. Tsuruko pull him around. At this time, his feelings were somewhat like drinking half a catty of aged Shaoxing wine, dizzy.

Amateur Musings

How to Organize Research 277

— Pu

In the past, this journal has published many articles about the bitterness of life. Several proposals for organization have appeared in the "Clerk Communications" section. Solving common bitterness through common organization is a legitimate path. We see that the current situation in North China is full of unpreparedness and disorganization. Compared with our enemies, it has become an inverse proportion. The reason is that the government organization is unsound, and the people lack a well-organized group to serve as the government's backing and to urge the government to improve the current situation. As a result, the national crisis is becoming increasingly serious. If we want to fulfill our responsibilities to the country, we should first study the issue of organization and experiment with it. Because we firmly believe that there is power in organization. When the masses are organized, they have power. Only then can a well-organized and powerful government be produced, can we resist organized imperialists, and can we save this unprecedented national crisis.

When it comes to the topic of "How to Organize," it seems to have a danger of reaction at first glance. In fact, if it is explained as how to unite, it will not be a problem. "Unity" is an empty noun, and its reality is organization. Unity is the result of organization; in other words, the result of organization is unity. It is not that the Chinese are not united, but because there is no organization. However, in today's China, the national spirit has been declining for a long time, and unity is extremely scattered. If we want to promote it once, we must have long-term training. Therefore, "organization" must have certain steps and must be done step by step in order to have good results. At the same time, we must also understand the difficulty of "organization." We must have great patience and great perseverance to do it in order to succeed. What must be eliminated most is the attitude of "wait and see." Everyone must be able to take responsibility.

To organize a group, to put it briefly, it is nothing more than the following main conditions:

㈠ Have a common goal. If the motive of an organization is based on individuals and seeks the interests of a few people, then the organization itself has no meaning at all. Therefore, in order to become a truly public and powerful group organization, we must first determine a common goal that truly seeks the interests of the public, and then study and formulate a plan for action in accordance with this common goal. Only then can actions tend to be consistent, and the spirit of the organization can be easily expressed.

㈡ Determine the source of economic income. Everyone knows the importance of economy. Many great undertakings have failed due to insufficient economic resources. Group organizations are no exception. Therefore, even if there is a spirit of perseverance and determination to work hard, the lack of economic power will make it difficult to implement concrete plans. Wouldn't it be a fatal flaw? Therefore, the source of economic income must be determined in order to reduce obstacles to progress.

㈢ Have a backbone group. The so-called backbone group is the basic members who can take responsibility in a group organization. Each basic member feels the bitterness of life and dissatisfaction with the status quo, and thus jointly unites into an organization. They have a deep understanding of the organization itself. Using their different environments, they proceed towards a common goal, without impatience, without disappointment, with perseverance and hard work. In this process, a outstanding leader will naturally emerge, overcoming all difficulties, never discouraged, and able to sacrifice oneself to achieve the public. Such as Lenin of Russia, Gandhi of India, and Mussolini of Italy, are such figures.

Although there are other conditions, it is not difficult to organize if the above three principles are met. However, in the current state of China, how should we organize to reform society? We now propose a simple step for reference:

㈠ Firmly establish a position and study the methods to start:

㈡ Initially, a small group should be organized by a few people who are responsible for it, and devote themselves to it with full interest and great perseverance, and prepare for the long term with a long-term vision, as a part of the foundation for future expansion of the organization:

㈢ Establish a step for publishing the plan;

㈣ The period of publicly soliciting members;

㈤ The period of simultaneous public and secret actions;

㈥ Pay attention to practical work and expand publicity period. At this point, it is almost a day when an organization has achieved considerable success.

The above six steps are all responsible for the mission of training the people, organizing the people, and educating the people. What those who participate need most is a firm spirit and practical action. The more failures, the more you must try. Only in this way can you gradually restore the people's national spirit and save the Republic of China from extinction!

Discussion of Issues

How to Make Merchants Follow the National Calendar for the New Year? 278

— Chen Jingyu

The Problem of Merchants Still Following the Lunar Calendar for the New Year

The decree to abolish the old calendar and adopt the national calendar was issued by the government to the whole country long ago, and several years have passed. However, most merchants mostly regard it as a dead letter and do not comply with it. Take Shanghai, a civilized city, as an example. Although some banks and stores can still close their doors for business during the National Calendar New Year, pretending to be celebrating the New Year, other ordinary stores still open their doors and do business. In fact, how can these stores that have never celebrated the New Year give up their long-inherited New Year customs and neglect rest? Then, since they don't celebrate the National Calendar New Year, they are naturally looking forward to the arrival of the lunar calendar New Year. When their hope is reached, they still close their doors and stop business as usual.

As for our countryside, they especially don't take the National Calendar seriously. No matter which store it is, every National Calendar New Year, they always trade as usual, without any sign of the New Year. But when the lunar calendar New Year arrives, everyone closes their doors in unison and the market stops. When acquaintances meet, they always raise their hands high and shout the slogans "Congratulations" and "Get Rich"! However, if you check their accounts, they are clearly written in the National Calendar year and month! If one corner is like this, it will be difficult to find exceptions elsewhere. This strange state of affairs, where the donkey's head doesn't match the horse's mouth, has become a deformed phenomenon in today's deformed society, with two New Years in a year!

Originally, the people have an absolute obligation to obey national laws and decrees; and the issuance of orders and the following of the law implies prestige. Therefore, if the country's laws and decrees are not implemented, its prestige will be swept away! Now, these merchants who think that the National Calendar is insignificant are always "stuck in the old ways" and do not change their old New Year customs. This is simply treating laws and decrees as trivial things, and regarding prestige as nothing. This gives the country the ridicule of "government orders not leaving the capital," which makes foreigners laugh! Such a lawless behavior that disregards the country's face should not be done by our so-called patriotic merchants! Therefore, it is necessary to follow the National Calendar for the New Year and implement it consistently! Considering the reason why they are unwilling to innovate, it is nothing more than an excuse that it hinders the collection of accounts at the end of the year. According to insiders, "The goods in the store are all purchased from Shanghai, and all transactions are recorded in accounts. The "Dragon Boat Festival," "Mid-Autumn Festival," and "Year-End" three festivals of the lunar calendar are the payment periods, especially the Year-End conclusion is the most important. They must be returned in full and no arrears are allowed. The place where the goods are sold is in the countryside, mostly on credit. The liquidation period is only the Year-End festival. Those people in the countryside all regard the end of the year as an unbreakable rule for repaying debts. They must bring the money to pay only when the end of the year is approaching; otherwise, no matter how hard you try to ask, they will ignore you. Once the National Calendar is followed and the New Year is celebrated earlier, the collection of debts will be even more troublesome. Since there is no income at this time, how can we deal with the Shanghai merchants? Therefore, for the New Year, we can only follow the lunar calendar." From this point of view, they are also clinging to the prevailing customs; therefore, they are getting by and unwilling to make more changes. In fact, if everyone can unanimously respect the National Calendar and wash away the traces of celebrating the lunar calendar New Year, then, when the National Calendar Year-End arrives, the people in the countryside will naturally rush to settle their accounts quickly, and there will be no reason to refuse to pay. You must know that customs can be changed by human effort, the problem is that you don't make an effort to do it! Therefore, the most important thing at present is what methods should be used to smash their stubborn prejudices, so that in the future, there will be hope of following the National Calendar for the New Year!

This issue is related to the overall situation of the country, not a small matter. Therefore, it is specially brought to this journal for public discussion. There is no shortage of enlightened people in the country. I hope you will not hesitate to give your valuable opinions! I will be very happy!

Life in the Business and Industry World

Bucket #62 279

— Li Yinghui

The Life of a Sweeping Worker in a Cotton Mill

In the weaving workshop of the ×× Cotton Mill, the machines are running, the young sisters are busy with their hands, and the workers are also doing their own work. Bucket #62 said to two sweeping workers:

"Fifty-seven, One hundred and eight, come to my house after noon tomorrow to help me move."

After saying that, he walked to the side. Naturally, what the bucket said is equivalent to giving an order, and not a request: because it is an order, it does not need their answer.

Fifty-seven and One hundred and eight raised their heads and looked at each other, said nothing, and then lowered their heads to sweep the messy thread ends again.

Bucket #62 walked to the side of the two workers again.

"Do you know my house, No. ××, Bolu Lane?" He said to them again; "Moving to No. 20, ×× Fang."

After telling them, he walked away, but immediately turned back and added two sentences: "Did you hear that, don't forget, go after noon tomorrow, don't come to the factory after noon."

× × × × × ×

When leaving work in the evening, Fifty-seven and One hundred and eight met outside the factory, each carrying a lunch box in their hands. Fifty-seven was about to take a rickshaw to Yangshupu Bridge when he saw One hundred and eight and asked first: "Where are you going, One hundred and eight?"

"Songpan Road Vegetable Market, where are you going?"

"Okay, let's go together, I won't take a rickshaw either, I'm going to Yangshupu Bridge, let's discuss tomorrow's business."

"Okay." Saying that, the two people slowly walked east along Yangshupu Road.

"I said don't go." Fifty-seven said.

"I don't want to go either, why help him move!"

"That's what I said. He usually oppresses the workers everywhere, hitting, scolding, fining, he does the most bad things, he is the workers' great enemy!"

"He is a great enemy, I said I won't help him move!"

"Don't move! It's really a mistake to help a running dog move."

"Helping an enemy move, you can't find one in the world!"

"Okay, then definitely don't go!"

"Definitely don't go!"

The matter was discussed. When they arrived at Yangshupu Bridge, Fifty-seven took a fork in Lan Road, One hundred and eight crossed the bridge and continued straight ahead, the two turned their heads and waved their hands far away.

× × × × × ×

Half a day passed again, and the whistle sounded, and the male and female workers of the ×× Cotton Mill ate lunch together. Everyone ate busily, and after a while, the whistle sounded again, and one after another they went back to the workshop to work. Fifty-seven and One hundred and eight were still working as usual in the weaving workshop, but Bucket #62 was not there.

Another half an hour passed. Suddenly, Bucket #62 walked there with a face full of anger. He sat down in the position he sat in every day, and he called Fifty-seven and One hundred and eight over.

"Why didn't you two go! Didn't you hear what I said yesterday? Are your ears growing in your mother's butt?" He scolded as soon as he opened his mouth.

The two people didn't say a word.

"Go, come with me, put down the brooms and leave!" After giving the order, he raised his butt to leave.

"Don't go." The two people said together.

Because he didn't make it, Bucket showed his power: "Why don't you go?"

"That's not my business."

"I didn't come here to help people move."

Bucket was so angry that his mouth was buzzing, and he couldn't speak for a while. After a long time, he couldn't help but say angrily:

"Okay, get out of here! If you don't go, it's like killing a pig and I won't eat a hairy pig!"

Although he said that, he didn't go back to help move after all, and sat back in his original seat, staring at the two people working. It looked like he would only relieve his hatred by nailing it into the hearts of the two workers.

× × × × × ×

Four days later, Fifty-seven and One hundred and eight were each fined one dollar, the reason "is that they are skimming the cream of the crop"!

Naturally, it is impossible for them to deal with a bucket alone, but they are so angry that they must do something!

"We must do something!"

"I have a way!"

Two days later, something really happened. All the workers and young sisters in the whole weaving workshop stopped working together to protest against the unreasonable oppression of workers by Bucket #62. In less than an hour, the writing room posted the following notice: "Bucket #62 is not doing his job well, he is ordered to stop working immediately."

Nineteen Years Old and Still Unmarried 281

｜Three Chapters of the Covenant｜

A certain gentleman is nineteen years old, from Hubei, unmarried, graduated from a certain middle school, and has served as a lecturer, editor of the editorial department, editor, teacher, assistant director, with both good character and appearance, proficient in Chinese (works are scattered in various newspapers and magazines) and has a little knowledge of English. Willing to serve as a literary editor, or elementary school teacher, or film actor, or driver. However, there are three prerequisites: ㈠ Not employed by the Japanese; ㈡ The employer must respect the employee's personality; ㈢ The salary must be able to maintain the living expenses of a family of six living in Shanghai (this condition can be compromised under certain circumstances). If you wish to hire, please send a letter to Zhang Zhengjun, Shanghai Student Dormitory, No. 30, Dexing Lane, Carter Road, this city.
